"""Fused W4A16 Kimi-Linear hybrid decode (batch=1).

Beats baseline.py by fusing the int4 unpack + per-group asymmetric dequant
directly into the GEMV (the weights are streamed once as int4, never
materialized to bf16), plus the MLA absorb reformulation so the latent KV cache
is never re-expanded through kv_b.
"""
from __future__ import annotations

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import torch.nn.functional as F
import triton
import triton.language as tl

EPS = 1.0e-6
GROUP = 128


# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
# Fused int4 dequant GEMV (batch=1), split-K, optional expert gather.
# y[e,n] = sum_k x[e_or_0,k] * (unpack(wq)[e,k,n] - zeros[e,k//G,n]) * scales[..]
# Using the group identity:
#   y = sum_g scales_g * ( sum_{k in g} x_k*w_k  -  zeros_g * sum_{k in g} x_k )
# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
def _gemv_configs():
    cfgs = []
    for BN in (32, 64, 128):
        for SK in (4, 8, 16):
            for nw in (1, 2):
                for ns in (2, 3, 4):
                    cfgs.append(triton.Config(
                        {"BLOCK_N": BN, "SPLIT_K": SK}, num_warps=nw, num_stages=ns))
    return cfgs


@triton.autotune(configs=_gemv_configs(), key=["N", "NG", "Eact"], reset_to_zero=["y_ptr"])
@triton.jit
def _gemv_kernel(
    x_ptr, wq_ptr, s_ptr, z_ptr, idx_ptr, y_ptr,
    K, N, NG, Eact,
    stride_xe, stride_xk,
    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
    stride_se, stride_sg, stride_sn,
    stride_ye, stride_yn,
    GROUP: tl.constexpr, USE_IDX: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, SPLIT_K: tl.constexpr,
):
    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_e = tl.program_id(1)
    pid_k = tl.program_id(2)
    if USE_IDX:
        e = tl.load(idx_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    else:
        e = pid_e
    n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    nmask = n < N
    wq_e = wq_ptr + e * stride_we
    s_e = s_ptr + e * stride_se
    z_e = z_ptr + e * stride_se
    x_e = x_ptr + pid_e * stride_xe
    acc = tl.zeros([BLOCK_N], dtype=tl.float32)
    HG: tl.constexpr = GROUP // 2
    rows = tl.arange(0, HG)
    for g in range(pid_k, NG, SPLIT_K):
        kp = g * HG + rows
        wq = tl.load(wq_e + kp[:, None] * stride_wk + n[None, :] * stride_wn,
                     mask=nmask[None, :], other=0)
        lo = (wq & 0xF).to(tl.float32)
        hi = ((wq >> 4) & 0xF).to(tl.float32)
        xe_ = tl.load(x_e + (2 * kp) * stride_xk)
        xo_ = tl.load(x_e + (2 * kp + 1) * stride_xk)
        raw = tl.sum(xe_[:, None] * lo + xo_[:, None] * hi, axis=0)
        xs = tl.sum(xe_ + xo_)
        s = tl.load(s_e + g * stride_sg + n * stride_sn, mask=nmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(z_e + g * stride_sg + n * stride_sn, mask=nmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc += s * (raw - z * xs)
    if SPLIT_K == 1:
        tl.store(y_ptr + pid_e * stride_ye + n * stride_yn, acc, mask=nmask)
    else:
        tl.atomic_add(y_ptr + pid_e * stride_ye + n * stride_yn, acc, mask=nmask)


def gemv(x, wq, scales, zeros, idx=None, out=None):
    """x:[K] (shared) or [Eact,K]; wq:[E,K//2,N] or [K//2,N]; -> [Eact,N] fp32."""
    if wq.dim() == 2:
        wq = wq.unsqueeze(0)
        scales = scales.unsqueeze(0)
        zeros = zeros.unsqueeze(0)
    E, Kp, N = wq.shape
    K = Kp * 2
    NG = scales.shape[1]
    use_idx = idx is not None
    Eact = idx.numel() if use_idx else E
    if x.dim() == 1:
        stride_xe, stride_xk = 0, x.stride(0)
    else:
        stride_xe, stride_xk = x.stride(0), x.stride(1)
    if out is None:
        out = torch.empty((Eact, N), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
    out.zero_()
    grid = lambda meta: (triton.cdiv(N, meta["BLOCK_N"]), Eact, meta["SPLIT_K"])
    _gemv_kernel[grid](
        x, wq, scales, zeros, idx if use_idx else x, out,
        K, N, NG, Eact,
        stride_xe, stride_xk,
        wq.stride(0), wq.stride(1), wq.stride(2),
        scales.stride(0), scales.stride(1), scales.stride(2),
        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
        GROUP=GROUP, USE_IDX=use_idx,
    )
    return out


@triton.autotune(configs=_gemv_configs(), key=["N", "NG", "Eact"], reset_to_zero=["y_ptr"])
@triton.jit
def _gemv_acc_kernel(
    x_ptr, wq_ptr, s_ptr, z_ptr, idx_ptr, sc_ptr, y_ptr,
    K, N, NG, Eact,
    stride_xe, stride_xk,
    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
    stride_se, stride_sg, stride_sn,
    GROUP: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, SPLIT_K: tl.constexpr,
):
    """Weighted accumulate GEMV: y[n] += scale[e] * sum_k x[e,k]*w[e,k,n], over all e."""
    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_e = tl.program_id(1)
    pid_k = tl.program_id(2)
    e = tl.load(idx_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
    sc = tl.load(sc_ptr + pid_e)
    n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    nmask = n < N
    wq_e = wq_ptr + e * stride_we
    s_e = s_ptr + e * stride_se
    z_e = z_ptr + e * stride_se
    x_e = x_ptr + pid_e * stride_xe
    acc = tl.zeros([BLOCK_N], dtype=tl.float32)
    HG: tl.constexpr = GROUP // 2
    rows = tl.arange(0, HG)
    for g in range(pid_k, NG, SPLIT_K):
        kp = g * HG + rows
        wq = tl.load(wq_e + kp[:, None] * stride_wk + n[None, :] * stride_wn,
                     mask=nmask[None, :], other=0)
        lo = (wq & 0xF).to(tl.float32)
        hi = ((wq >> 4) & 0xF).to(tl.float32)
        xe_ = tl.load(x_e + (2 * kp) * stride_xk)
        xo_ = tl.load(x_e + (2 * kp + 1) * stride_xk)
        raw = tl.sum(xe_[:, None] * lo + xo_[:, None] * hi, axis=0)
        xs = tl.sum(xe_ + xo_)
        s = tl.load(s_e + g * stride_sg + n * stride_sn, mask=nmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(z_e + g * stride_sg + n * stride_sn, mask=nmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc += s * (raw - z * xs)
    tl.atomic_add(y_ptr + n, sc * acc, mask=nmask)


def gemv_acc(x, wq, scales, zeros, idx, scale, out):
    """x:[Eact,K]; accumulate scale[e]*(x[e]@dequant(wq[idx[e]])) into out[N]."""
    E, Kp, N = wq.shape
    K = Kp * 2
    NG = scales.shape[1]
    Eact = idx.numel()
    out.zero_()
    grid = lambda meta: (triton.cdiv(N, meta["BLOCK_N"]), Eact, meta["SPLIT_K"])
    _gemv_acc_kernel[grid](
        x, wq, scales, zeros, idx, scale, out,
        K, N, NG, Eact,
        x.stride(0), x.stride(1),
        wq.stride(0), wq.stride(1), wq.stride(2),
        scales.stride(0), scales.stride(1), scales.stride(2),
        GROUP=GROUP,
    )
    return out


@triton.jit
def _router_logits_kernel(x_ptr, w_ptr, out_ptr, D, BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr):
    """One program per expert: logit[e] = sum_d x[d] * W[e,d].
    x rounded to bf16 to match the reference's bf16 router (keeps top-k selection identical)."""
    e = tl.program_id(0)
    acc = tl.zeros([BLOCK_D], dtype=tl.float32)
    for d0 in range(0, D, BLOCK_D):
        dd = d0 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_D)
        dm = dd < D
        xv = tl.load(x_ptr + dd, mask=dm, other=0.0).to(tl.bfloat16).to(tl.float32)
        acc += xv * tl.load(w_ptr + e * D + dd, mask=dm, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    tl.store(out_ptr + e, tl.sum(acc, 0))


@triton.jit
def _router_topk_kernel(
    logits_ptr, idxg_ptr, idxgu_ptr, scale_ptr,
    E, scaling, GATE_OFF,
    NACT: tl.constexpr, NS: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_E: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_J: tl.constexpr,
):
    """top-k(logits) + softmax + gather-index build (one program).
    Emits idx_g[NACT+NS], idx_gu[2*(NACT+NS)] (gate then up), scale[NACT+NS]."""
    e = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_E)
    emask = e < E
    logits = tl.where(emask, tl.load(logits_ptr + e, mask=emask, other=0.0), -float("inf"))
    jr = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_J)
    idx_vec = tl.zeros([BLOCK_J], dtype=tl.int32)
    val_vec = tl.full([BLOCK_J], -float("inf"), dtype=tl.float32)
    for j in range(NACT):
        mx = tl.max(logits, 0)
        am = tl.argmax(logits, 0).to(tl.int32)
        idx_vec = tl.where(jr == j, am, idx_vec)
        val_vec = tl.where(jr == j, mx, val_vec)
        logits = tl.where(e == am, -float("inf"), logits)
    idx_vec = tl.where(jr == NACT, E, idx_vec)               # shared expert at slot NACT
    routed = jr < NACT
    vmax = tl.max(tl.where(routed, val_vec, -float("inf")), 0)
    ev = tl.where(routed, tl.exp(val_vec - vmax), 0.0)
    sm = ev / tl.sum(ev, 0) * scaling
    scale_vec = tl.where(routed, sm, tl.where(jr == NACT, 1.0, 0.0))
    ns_mask = jr < (NACT + NS)
    tl.store(idxg_ptr + jr, idx_vec, mask=ns_mask)
    tl.store(scale_ptr + jr, scale_vec, mask=ns_mask)
    tl.store(idxgu_ptr + jr, idx_vec, mask=ns_mask)
    tl.store(idxgu_ptr + (NACT + NS) + jr, idx_vec + GATE_OFF, mask=ns_mask)


def router_topk(x, w, n_active, n_shared, gate_off, scaling, E, logits_buf):
    dev = x.device
    ns = n_active + n_shared
    idx_g = torch.empty(ns, device=dev, dtype=torch.int32)
    idx_gu = torch.empty(2 * ns, device=dev, dtype=torch.int32)
    scale = torch.empty(ns, device=dev, dtype=torch.float32)
    D = x.shape[-1]
    _router_logits_kernel[(E,)](x, w, logits_buf, D, BLOCK_D=triton.next_power_of_2(D))
    _router_topk_kernel[(1,)](
        logits_buf, idx_g, idx_gu, scale, E, scaling, gate_off,
        NACT=n_active, NS=n_shared,
        BLOCK_E=triton.next_power_of_2(E), BLOCK_J=triton.next_power_of_2(ns),
    )
    return idx_g, idx_gu, scale


@triton.jit
def _silu_mul_kernel(g_ptr, u_ptr, o_ptr, n_elem, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
    pid = tl.program_id(0)
    off = pid * BLOCK + tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
    m = off < n_elem
    g = tl.load(g_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0)
    u = tl.load(u_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0)
    tl.store(o_ptr + off, (g * tl.sigmoid(g)) * u, mask=m)


def silu_mul(g, u):
    o = torch.empty_like(g)
    n = g.numel()
    _silu_mul_kernel[(triton.cdiv(n, 1024),)](g, u, o, n, BLOCK=1024)
    return o


@triton.jit
def _kda_conv_kernel(
    qkv_ptr, cw_ptr, st_ptr, out_ptr, C,
    scw_t, scw_n, scw_k, BLOCK: tl.constexpr,
):
    """Depthwise causal conv (kernel 4) + SiLU on q/k/v, with in-place ring shift.
    qkv_ptr: [>=3, C] (rows q,k,v); st_ptr: [3,3,C] window state; out_ptr: [3,C]."""
    pid_t = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    n = pid_n * BLOCK + tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
    m = n < C
    val = tl.load(qkv_ptr + pid_t * C + n, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    cw = cw_ptr + pid_t * scw_t + n * scw_n
    w0 = tl.load(cw + 0 * scw_k, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w1 = tl.load(cw + 1 * scw_k, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w2 = tl.load(cw + 2 * scw_k, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w3 = tl.load(cw + 3 * scw_k, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    sb = st_ptr + pid_t * 3 * C + n
    s0 = tl.load(sb + 0 * C, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    s1 = tl.load(sb + 1 * C, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    s2 = tl.load(sb + 2 * C, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    acc = s0 * w0 + s1 * w1 + s2 * w2 + val * w3
    tl.store(out_ptr + pid_t * C + n, acc * tl.sigmoid(acc), mask=m)
    tl.store(sb + 0 * C, s1.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=m)
    tl.store(sb + 1 * C, s2.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=m)
    tl.store(sb + 2 * C, val.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=m)


def kda_conv(qkv, conv_w, state):
    """qkv:[>=3,C]; conv_w:[3,C,4]; state:[3,3,C] bf16 (in place). -> out:[3,C] fp32."""
    C = qkv.shape[1]
    out = torch.empty((3, C), device=qkv.device, dtype=torch.float32)
    grid = (3, triton.cdiv(C, 1024))
    _kda_conv_kernel[grid](
        qkv, conv_w, state, out, C,
        conv_w.stride(0), conv_w.stride(1), conv_w.stride(2), BLOCK=1024,
    )
    return out


@triton.jit
def _kda_recur_kernel(
    S_ptr, q_ptr, k_ptr, v_ptr, g_ptr, beta_ptr, o_ptr,
    stride_sh, stride_sk, stride_sv, scale,
    DK: tl.constexpr, DV: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_V: tl.constexpr,
):
    pid_h = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_v = tl.program_id(1)
    koff = tl.arange(0, DK)
    voff = pid_v * BLOCK_V + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_V)
    key = tl.load(k_ptr + pid_h * DK + koff)
    qry = tl.load(q_ptr + pid_h * DK + koff) * scale
    graw = tl.load(g_ptr + pid_h * DK + koff)
    decay = tl.sigmoid(-graw)                              # = exp(-softplus(graw))
    beta = tl.load(beta_ptr + pid_h)
    val = tl.load(v_ptr + pid_h * DV + voff)
    sbase = S_ptr + pid_h * stride_sh + koff[:, None] * stride_sk + voff[None, :] * stride_sv
    S = tl.load(sbase)
    Sd = S * decay[:, None]
    pred = tl.sum(Sd * key[:, None], axis=0)
    Snew = Sd + (beta * key)[:, None] * (val - pred)[None, :]
    o = tl.sum(Snew * qry[:, None], axis=0)
    tl.store(sbase, Snew)
    tl.store(o_ptr + pid_h * DV + voff, o)


def kda_recur(S, q, k, v, g_raw, beta, scale, BLOCK_V=64):
    """S:[H,DK,DV] fp32 in place; q,k,v,g_raw:[H,DK]; beta:[H]. q scaled, decay=sigmoid(-g_raw)."""
    H, DK, DV = S.shape
    o = torch.empty((H, DV), device=S.device, dtype=torch.float32)
    grid = (H, triton.cdiv(DV, BLOCK_V))
    _kda_recur_kernel[grid](
        S, q, k, v, g_raw, beta, o,
        S.stride(0), S.stride(1), S.stride(2), scale,
        DK=DK, DV=DV, BLOCK_V=BLOCK_V,
    )
    return o


def _unpack_dequant(wq, scales, zeros, group=GROUP):
    """Dequant a single [K//2,N] int4 weight to [K,N] bf16 (only used for kv_b)."""
    Kp, N = wq.shape
    wu = torch.empty((2 * Kp, N), dtype=torch.uint8, device=wq.device)
    wu[0::2] = wq & 0xF
    wu[1::2] = (wq >> 4) & 0xF
    s = scales.repeat_interleave(group, dim=0)
    z = zeros.repeat_interleave(group, dim=0)
    return (wu.to(torch.bfloat16) - z) * s


# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
# modules (buffer/param names identical to reference for state_dict load)
# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
class QuantLinear(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, in_f, out_f, group=GROUP):
        super().__init__()
        self.in_f, self.out_f, self.group = in_f, out_f, group
        ng = in_f // group
        self.register_buffer("w_q", torch.zeros(in_f // 2, out_f, dtype=torch.uint8))
        self.register_buffer("scales", torch.zeros(ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
        self.register_buffer("zeros", torch.zeros(ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))


class QuantExperts(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, n, in_f, out_f, group=GROUP):
        super().__init__()
        self.n, self.in_f, self.out_f, self.group = n, in_f, out_f, group
        ng = in_f // group
        self.register_buffer("w_q", torch.zeros(n, in_f // 2, out_f, dtype=torch.uint8))
        self.register_buffer("scales", torch.zeros(n, ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
        self.register_buffer("zeros", torch.zeros(n, ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))


@triton.jit
def _rmsnorm_kernel(x_ptr, w_ptr, o_ptr, N: tl.constexpr, eps, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
    off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
    m = off < N
    x = tl.load(x_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w = tl.load(w_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    r = tl.rsqrt(tl.sum(x * x) / N + eps)
    tl.store(o_ptr + off, x * r * w, mask=m)


def _rmsnorm(x, w):
    """Fused RMSNorm; returns fp32 (ready for the dequant-GEMV)."""
    N = x.shape[-1]
    o = torch.empty(N, device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
    BLOCK = triton.next_power_of_2(N)
    _rmsnorm_kernel[(1,)](x, w, o, N, EPS, BLOCK=BLOCK)
    return o


@triton.jit
def _rmsnorm_add_kernel(x_ptr, y_ptr, w_ptr, resid_ptr, o_ptr, N: tl.constexpr, eps, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
    off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
    m = off < N
    # round y to bf16 before the add to match reference's bf16 residual exactly
    yb = tl.load(y_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.bfloat16).to(tl.float32)
    s = tl.load(x_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32) + yb
    sb = s.to(tl.bfloat16)
    tl.store(resid_ptr + off, sb, mask=m)
    sf = sb.to(tl.float32)                          # match reference: norm the bf16 residual
    r = tl.rsqrt(tl.sum(sf * sf) / N + eps)
    w = tl.load(w_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    tl.store(o_ptr + off, sf * r * w, mask=m)


def _rmsnorm_add(x, y, w):
    """resid = x + y (bf16); returns (resid, rmsnorm(resid) fp32)."""
    N = x.shape[-1]
    resid = torch.empty(N, device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    o = torch.empty(N, device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
    _rmsnorm_add_kernel[(1,)](x, y, w, resid, o, N, EPS, BLOCK=triton.next_power_of_2(N))
    return resid, o


def _rope_cossin(pos, dim, theta, device):
    inv = 1.0 / (theta ** (torch.arange(0, dim, 2, device=device, dtype=torch.float32) / dim))
    ang = pos * inv
    return torch.cos(ang), torch.sin(ang)


def _apply_rope(x, cos, sin):
    xf = x.float()
    even, odd = xf[..., 0::2], xf[..., 1::2]
    out = torch.empty_like(xf)
    out[..., 0::2] = even * cos - odd * sin
    out[..., 1::2] = odd * cos + even * sin
    return out.to(x.dtype)


class KDA(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        H, Dk, d = cfg.kda_heads, cfg.kda_head_dim, cfg.hidden
        self.q_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.k_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.v_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.g_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.beta_proj = nn.Linear(d, H, bias=False, dtype=cfg.dtype)
        self.conv_w = nn.Parameter(torch.empty(3, H * Dk, cfg.short_conv, dtype=cfg.dtype))
        self.o_proj = QuantLinear(H * Dk, d, cfg.group)
        self.scale = Dk ** -0.5

    def _stack(self):
        self._wq = torch.stack([self.q_proj.w_q, self.k_proj.w_q,
                                self.v_proj.w_q, self.g_proj.w_q])
        self._s = torch.stack([self.q_proj.scales, self.k_proj.scales,
                               self.v_proj.scales, self.g_proj.scales])
        self._z = torch.stack([self.q_proj.zeros, self.k_proj.zeros,
                               self.v_proj.zeros, self.g_proj.zeros])

    def _conv(self, val, prev, idx):
        # val:[C] fp32, prev:[3,C] bf16, conv_w[idx]:[C,4]
        win = torch.cat([prev.float(), val[None]], dim=0)      # [4,C]
        w = self.conv_w[idx].float().transpose(0, 1)            # [4,C]
        out = F.silu((win * w).sum(0))                          # [C]
        return out, win[1:].to(prev.dtype)

    def step(self, x, st):
        H, Dk = self.cfg.kda_heads, self.cfg.kda_head_dim
        if not hasattr(self, "_wq"):
            self._stack()
        xf = x.float()
        qkvg = gemv(xf, self._wq, self._s, self._z)            # [4, H*Dk]
        q, st["cq"] = self._conv(qkvg[0], st["cq"], 0)
        k, st["ck"] = self._conv(qkvg[1], st["ck"], 1)
        v, st["cv"] = self._conv(qkvg[2], st["cv"], 2)
        q = q.view(H, Dk).contiguous()
        k = k.view(H, Dk).contiguous()
        v = v.view(H, Dk).contiguous()
        g_raw = qkvg[3].view(H, Dk).contiguous()
        beta = torch.sigmoid(self.beta_proj(x.to(torch.bfloat16)).float()).contiguous()
        o = kda_recur(st["S"], q, k, v, g_raw, beta, self.scale)   # updates S in place
        of = o.reshape(H * Dk)
        return gemv(of, self.o_proj.w_q, self.o_proj.scales, self.o_proj.zeros).squeeze(0)

    def step_g(self, x, S_buf, conv_state):
        H, Dk = self.cfg.kda_heads, self.cfg.kda_head_dim
        if not hasattr(self, "_wq"):
            self._stack()
        xf = x.float()
        qkvg = gemv(xf, self._wq, self._s, self._z)                # [4, C]
        conv_out = kda_conv(qkvg, self.conv_w, conv_state)         # [3, C], state updated
        beta = torch.sigmoid(self.beta_proj(x.to(torch.bfloat16)).float())
        o = kda_recur(S_buf, conv_out[0], conv_out[1], conv_out[2], qkvg[3], beta, self.scale)
        of = o.reshape(H * Dk)
        return gemv(of, self.o_proj.w_q, self.o_proj.scales, self.o_proj.zeros).squeeze(0)


class MLA(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        H, d = cfg.mla_heads, cfg.hidden
        self.q_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope), cfg.group)
        self.kv_a = QuantLinear(d, cfg.kv_lora + cfg.qk_rope, cfg.group)
        self.kv_b = QuantLinear(cfg.kv_lora, H * (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.v_head), cfg.group)
        self.o_proj = QuantLinear(H * cfg.v_head, d, cfg.group)
        self.scale = (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope) ** -0.5

    def _prep(self):
        cfg = self.cfg
        H, nope, vh, lora = cfg.mla_heads, cfg.qk_nope, cfg.v_head, cfg.kv_lora
        W = _unpack_dequant(self.kv_b.w_q, self.kv_b.scales, self.kv_b.zeros).view(lora, H, nope + vh)
        # per-head absorb matrices, bf16 for tensor-core matmuls
        self._Wkn = W[:, :, :nope].permute(1, 0, 2).contiguous()   # [H,512,nope]
        self._Wvn = W[:, :, nope:].permute(1, 0, 2).contiguous()   # [H,512,vh]
        dev = self.kv_b.w_q.device
        self._inv = 1.0 / (cfg.rope_theta ** (torch.arange(0, cfg.qk_rope, 2, device=dev, dtype=torch.float32) / cfg.qk_rope))
        # combined q_proj || kv_a (same input x); split output at qsplit
        self._qkva_wq = torch.cat([self.q_proj.w_q, self.kv_a.w_q], dim=1)
        self._qkva_s = torch.cat([self.q_proj.scales, self.kv_a.scales], dim=1)
        self._qkva_z = torch.cat([self.q_proj.zeros, self.kv_a.zeros], dim=1)
        self._qsplit = H * (nope + cfg.qk_rope)

    def step(self, x, st):
        cfg = self.cfg
        H = cfg.mla_heads
        nope, rope, vh, lora = cfg.qk_nope, cfg.qk_rope, cfg.v_head, cfg.kv_lora
        if not hasattr(self, "_Wkn"):
            self._prep()
        pos = st["c_kv"].shape[0]
        xf = x.float()
        qkva = gemv(xf, self._qkva_wq, self._qkva_s, self._qkva_z).squeeze(0)
        q = qkva[:self._qsplit].view(H, nope + rope)
        q_nope = q[:, :nope]
        q_rope = q[:, nope:]
        kv = qkva[self._qsplit:]
        c_kv = kv[:lora].to(torch.bfloat16)
        k_rope = kv[lora:]
        cos, sin = _rope_cossin(pos, rope, cfg.rope_theta, x.device)
        q_rope = _apply_rope(q_rope, cos, sin).to(torch.bfloat16)
        k_rope = _apply_rope(k_rope, cos, sin).to(torch.bfloat16)
        st["c_kv"] = torch.cat([st["c_kv"], c_kv[None]], 0)
        st["k_rope"] = torch.cat([st["k_rope"], k_rope[None]], 0)
        ckv = st["c_kv"]                                           # [L,512] bf16
        krope = st["k_rope"]                                       # [L,64] bf16
        # absorb q into latent space (per-head [512,nope] @ [nope] -> [512])
        q_absorb = torch.einsum("hdc,hc->hd", self._Wkn, q_nope.to(torch.bfloat16))  # [H,512] bf16
        scores = (q_absorb @ ckv.t() + q_rope @ krope.t()).float() * self.scale       # [H,L]
        p = torch.softmax(scores, dim=-1).to(torch.bfloat16)                          # [H,L]
        pc = p @ ckv                                                                   # [H,512] bf16
        o = torch.einsum("hd,hdc->hc", pc, self._Wvn)                                  # [H,vh] bf16
        of = o.reshape(H * vh).float()
        return gemv(of, self.o_proj.w_q, self.o_proj.scales, self.o_proj.zeros).squeeze(0)

    def step_g(self, x, c_kv_buf, k_rope_buf, pos, maxlen):
        """Graph variant: pos is a [1] int64 GPU scalar; cache written in place at pos."""
        cfg = self.cfg
        H = cfg.mla_heads
        nope, rope, vh, lora = cfg.qk_nope, cfg.qk_rope, cfg.v_head, cfg.kv_lora
        if not hasattr(self, "_Wkn"):
            self._prep()
        xf = x.float()
        qkva = gemv(xf, self._qkva_wq, self._qkva_s, self._qkva_z).squeeze(0)
        q = qkva[:self._qsplit].view(H, nope + rope)
        q_nope = q[:, :nope]
        q_rope = q[:, nope:]
        kv = qkva[self._qsplit:]
        c_kv_new = kv[:lora].to(torch.bfloat16)
        k_rope_new = kv[lora:]
        inv = self._inv
        ang = pos.float() * inv                                  # [rope/2]
        cos, sin = torch.cos(ang), torch.sin(ang)
        q_rope = _apply_rope(q_rope, cos, sin).to(torch.bfloat16)
        k_rope_new = _apply_rope(k_rope_new, cos, sin).to(torch.bfloat16)
        c_kv_buf.index_copy_(0, pos, c_kv_new[None])
        k_rope_buf.index_copy_(0, pos, k_rope_new[None])
        q_absorb = torch.einsum("hdc,hc->hd", self._Wkn, q_nope.to(torch.bfloat16))    # [H,512]
        scores = (q_absorb @ c_kv_buf.t() + q_rope @ k_rope_buf.t()).float() * self.scale  # [H,maxlen]
        mask = torch.arange(maxlen, device=x.device) > pos
        scores = scores.masked_fill(mask[None, :], float("-inf"))
        p = torch.softmax(scores, dim=-1).to(torch.bfloat16)
        pc = p @ c_kv_buf
        o = torch.einsum("hd,hdc->hc", pc, self._Wvn)
        of = o.reshape(H * vh).float()
        return gemv(of, self.o_proj.w_q, self.o_proj.scales, self.o_proj.zeros).squeeze(0)


class MoE(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        d, m, E = cfg.hidden, cfg.moe_inter, cfg.n_experts
        self.router = nn.Linear(d, E, bias=False, dtype=cfg.dtype)
        self.gate = QuantExperts(E, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.up = QuantExperts(E, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.down = QuantExperts(E, m, d, cfg.group)
        self.s_gate = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.s_up = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.s_down = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, m, d, cfg.group)

    def _prep(self):
        dev = self.gate.w_q.device
        # combined routed+shared expert weights: index E (=n_experts) is the shared expert
        E = self.cfg.n_experts
        # combined gate||up weights: rows [gate(E), s_gate(1), up(E), s_up(1)]
        self._gu_wq = torch.cat([self.gate.w_q, self.s_gate.w_q, self.up.w_q, self.s_up.w_q], 0)
        self._gu_s = torch.cat([self.gate.scales, self.s_gate.scales, self.up.scales, self.s_up.scales], 0)
        self._gu_z = torch.cat([self.gate.zeros, self.s_gate.zeros, self.up.zeros, self.s_up.zeros], 0)
        self._d_wq = torch.cat([self.down.w_q, self.s_down.w_q], 0)
        self._d_s = torch.cat([self.down.scales, self.s_down.scales], 0)
        self._d_z = torch.cat([self.down.zeros, self.s_down.zeros], 0)
        self._gate_off = E + 1                                            # up block offset in gu
        self._out = torch.empty(self.cfg.hidden, device=dev, dtype=torch.float32)
        self._logits = torch.empty(E, device=dev, dtype=torch.float32)

    def step(self, x):
        cfg = self.cfg
        if not hasattr(self, "_gu_wq"):
            self._prep()
        ns = cfg.n_active + cfg.n_shared
        xf = x.float()
        idx_g, idx_gu, scale = router_topk(
            xf, self.router.weight, cfg.n_active, cfg.n_shared,
            self._gate_off, cfg.routed_scaling, cfg.n_experts, self._logits)
        gu = gemv(xf, self._gu_wq, self._gu_s, self._gu_z, idx=idx_gu)   # [2*ns, m]
        h = silu_mul(gu[:ns], gu[ns:])                                    # [ns, m]
        gemv_acc(h, self._d_wq, self._d_s, self._d_z, idx_g, scale, self._out)
        return self._out


class Block(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg, kind):
        super().__init__()
        self.kind = kind
        self.attn_norm = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(cfg.hidden, dtype=cfg.dtype))
        self.moe_norm = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(cfg.hidden, dtype=cfg.dtype))
        self.attn = KDA(cfg) if kind == "K" else MLA(cfg)
        self.moe = MoE(cfg)

    def step(self, x, st):
        h = x + self.attn.step(_rmsnorm(x, self.attn_norm), st)
        return h + self.moe.step(_rmsnorm(h, self.moe_norm))


HEADROOM = 256


class _Bundle:
    """Persistent buffers + captured CUDA graph for one context length."""
    __slots__ = ("maxlen", "h_in", "h_out", "pos", "cpos", "S", "conv",
                 "c_kv", "k_rope", "graph", "mla_idx")


class Model(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        self.blocks = nn.ModuleList(Block(cfg, k) for k in cfg.pattern)
        self._graphs = {}
        self._use_graph = True

    # ---- eager reference path (always correct) ---------------------------- #
    def _step_eager(self, hidden, state):
        for i, blk in enumerate(self.blocks):
            hidden = blk.step(hidden, state[i])
        return hidden, state

    # ---- graph machinery -------------------------------------------------- #
    def _forward_graph(self, b: _Bundle):
        ki = 0
        resid, add = b.h_in, None         # deferred residual: actual stream = resid + add
        for i, blk in enumerate(self.blocks):
            if add is None:
                xn = _rmsnorm(resid, blk.attn_norm)
            else:
                resid, xn = _rmsnorm_add(resid, add, blk.attn_norm)   # fold prev moe-residual add
            if blk.kind == "K":
                a = blk.attn.step_g(xn, b.S[ki], b.conv[ki])
                ki += 1
            else:
                a = blk.attn.step_g(xn, b.c_kv, b.k_rope, b.pos, b.maxlen)
            resid, xn2 = _rmsnorm_add(resid, a, blk.moe_norm)         # fold attn-residual add
            add = blk.moe.step(xn2)
        b.h_out.copy_(resid + add.to(torch.bfloat16))
        b.pos.add_(1)

    def _make_bundle(self, ctx, device):
        cfg = self.cfg
        H, Dk = cfg.kda_heads, cfg.kda_head_dim
        C = H * Dk
        b = _Bundle()
        b.maxlen = ctx + HEADROOM
        b.h_in = torch.zeros(cfg.hidden, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        b.h_out = torch.zeros(cfg.hidden, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        b.pos = torch.zeros(1, device=device, dtype=torch.int64)
        nk = sum(1 for k in cfg.pattern if k == "K")
        b.S = [torch.zeros(H, Dk, Dk, device=device, dtype=torch.float32) for _ in range(nk)]
        b.conv = [torch.zeros(3, 3, C, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16) for _ in range(nk)]
        b.c_kv = torch.zeros(b.maxlen, cfg.kv_lora, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        b.k_rope = torch.zeros(b.maxlen, cfg.qk_rope, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        b.mla_idx = cfg.pattern.index("M")
        return b

    def _capture(self, ctx, device):
        b = self._make_bundle(ctx, device)
        b.pos.fill_(ctx)
        s = torch.cuda.Stream()
        s.wait_stream(torch.cuda.current_stream())
        with torch.cuda.stream(s):
            for _ in range(3):
                self._forward_graph(b)
        torch.cuda.current_stream().wait_stream(s)
        torch.cuda.synchronize()
        b.graph = torch.cuda.CUDAGraph()
        with torch.cuda.graph(b.graph):
            self._forward_graph(b)
        self._graphs[ctx] = b
        return b

    def _load_state(self, b, state, ctx):
        """Copy a fresh dict state into bundle buffers; rebind dict to buffer views."""
        ki = 0
        for i, blk in enumerate(self.blocks):
            st = state[i]
            if blk.kind == "K":
                b.S[ki].copy_(st["S"])
                b.conv[ki][0].copy_(st["cq"]); b.conv[ki][1].copy_(st["ck"]); b.conv[ki][2].copy_(st["cv"])
                st["S"] = b.S[ki]
                st["cq"] = b.conv[ki][0]; st["ck"] = b.conv[ki][1]; st["cv"] = b.conv[ki][2]
                ki += 1
            else:
                b.c_kv[:ctx].copy_(st["c_kv"]); b.k_rope[:ctx].copy_(st["k_rope"])
                st["c_kv"] = b.c_kv[:ctx]; st["k_rope"] = b.k_rope[:ctx]
        b.pos.fill_(ctx)
        b.cpos = ctx

    def step(self, hidden, state):
        if not self._use_graph or not hidden.is_cuda:
            return self._step_eager(hidden, state)
        mla_idx = self.cfg.pattern.index("M")
        ckv = state[mla_idx]["c_kv"]
        try:
            b = self._cur if getattr(self, "_cur", None) is not None else None
            is_cont = (b is not None and ckv.data_ptr() == b.c_kv.data_ptr())
            if is_cont and b.cpos + 1 >= b.maxlen:        # cache overflow: drop to eager
                self._use_graph = False
                return self._step_eager(hidden, state)
            if not is_cont:
                ctx = ckv.shape[0]
                b = self._graphs.get(ctx) or self._capture(ctx, hidden.device)
                self._load_state(b, state, ctx)
                self._cur = b
            b.h_in.copy_(hidden)
            b.graph.replay()
            b.cpos += 1
            p = b.cpos
            state[mla_idx]["c_kv"] = b.c_kv[:p]
            state[mla_idx]["k_rope"] = b.k_rope[:p]
            return b.h_out, state
        except Exception:
            self._use_graph = False
            self._cur = None
            return self._step_eager(hidden, state)
Final result confirmed: **~19.2× geomean speedup** (18.5× / 19.0× / 20.2× over context lengths 2048 / 8192 / 16384), stable across runs, `check.py` PASS. Done. ## Summary I built `solution.py` — a fused W4A16 Kimi-Linear hybrid decode kernel that runs at **~0.46–0.49 ms/tok (~2100 tok/s), ~19× faster than `baseline.py`**, passing `check.py` (cosine ≥ 0.9947, well above the 0.98 gate). The GPU is actually a **B200** (Blackwell, ~6–7 TB/s), so this decode is dominated by per-kernel launch/floor overhead, not just raw bandwidth. The optimizations, in order of impact: **Core requirement — fused int4 dequant-GEMV (Triton):** streams the int4 weights once and fuses unpack + per-group asymmetric dequant directly into the GEMV using the group identity `y = Σ_g s_g·(Σ x·w − z_g·Σx)`, with split-K + atomics and autotuned configs. Never materializes the bf16 weight (2.5× faster than torch's bf16 GEMV per effective weight, at ¼ the bytes). **MLA absorb:** precompute the `kv_b` dequant **once** into per-head bf16 matrices; reformulate so the latent cache is never re-expanded, and keep scores as `[H, L]` so softmax is over the contiguous last dim (the reference's `softmax(dim=0)` over the strided 16k axis was 1.1 ms/step alone). **CUDA graphs (biggest single win, 3.4×→7.2×):** fixed-size MLA cache buffer + GPU `pos` scalar (masked attention, in-place `index_copy_`), eliminating ~1.4 ms/step of CPU launch overhead. New-run detection by `data_ptr`; eager fallback verified correct. **Aggressive fusion** of everything else: gated-delta recurrence kernel (with `exp(-softplus)=sigmoid(-x)` folded in), depthwise conv kernel, RMSNorm-fused-with-residual-add, combined gate‖up and q_proj‖kv_a GEMVs, weighted-accumulate down-projection, and a fused router top-k that emits gather indices directly. The remaining bottleneck is the int4 GEMV stream itself (~217 µs, 50% of the step) — floor-bound on 16 sequentially-dependent kernels. Going further would require a single persistent megakernel with grid-wide sync, which I judged too high-risk for the marginal gain given the already-strong, robust result.

1	I need you to make batch-1 autoregressive decode of a Kimi-Linear hybrid block as fast as possible on the RTX PRO 6000 (SM120 Blackwell, GDDR7, 1.8 TB/s). The model is W4A16: the big projection weights are stored as 4-bit integers, the activations and accumulation are bf16. reference.py is the correctness oracle and baseline.py is an already-optimized pure-PyTorch version; your job is to go beyond baseline.py. Your answer goes in solution.py and must expose the same Model class and the same step(hidden, state) -> (hidden, state) interface as reference.py, with identical buffer/parameter names so it loads the reference weights. Make whatever mess you want in this directory otherwise.
2	
3	The unit is one repeating motif of Kimi-Linear-48B-A3B: four layers in the pattern [KDA, KDA, KDA, MLA], each followed by a 64-expert MoE FFN (top-8 routed + 1 shared, SiLU, intermediate 1024), with RMSNorm and residuals. Hidden size is 2304. The KDA layers are gated-delta linear attention with 32 heads of dim 128, a short causal depthwise conv (kernel 4) on q/k/v, a per-channel log-decay gate, and a per-head write strength; they carry a fixed-size recurrent state S[32,128,128] plus the conv window across decode steps. The MLA layers are multi-head latent attention with 32 heads, a kv_lora_rank of 512, qk_nope 128, qk_rope 64, v_head 128, decoupled RoPE (theta 10000); they carry a growing compressed latent KV cache (the 512-d latent plus the 64-d rope key per past token).
4

1	"""PyTorch reference for a Kimi-Linear W4A16 hybrid decode unit (batch=1).
2	
3	Correctness oracle, NOT the fast baseline (baseline.py) or the SOTA ceiling.
4	One repeating motif of Kimi-Linear-48B-A3B -- 3 KDA (gated-delta linear attn)
5	layers + 1 MLA (multi-head latent attention) layer, each + a 64-expert MoE FFN
6	-- decoded one token at a time, with the big projection weights stored as
7	**W4A16** (int4 weights, group-128 asymmetric, bf16 accumulation; the AWQ/GPTQ
8	format that open-source inference actually ships).
9	
10	Why W4A16 and not fp8: at batch-1 decode the bottleneck is *weight memory
11	traffic*. int4 weights are 0.25x the bytes of bf16 (4x less traffic), and a
12	fused dequant-GEMV realizes that win in the memory-bound regime where decode
13	lives -- unlike fp8 tensor-core matmul, which has fixed overhead and loses at
14	M=1. int4/bf16-acc also needs no special tensor-core format, so it runs on any
15	bf16-capable GPU (Ampere, Hopper, Blackwell).
16	
17	The two decode states are unchanged: KDA carries a fixed-size recurrent state
18	S[H,Dk,Dv] + short-conv window; MLA carries a growing compressed latent KV
19	cache. `step(hidden, state) -> (hidden, state)` consumes one token.
20	
21	This reference dequantizes naively (unpack -> bf16 matrix -> matmul). The whole
22	problem is to FUSE the int4 unpack+dequant into the GEMV and never materialize
23	the bf16 weight. Pack format is identical to KernelBench-Hard problem 07.
24	
25	Contract (reference.py / baselin

1	"""Latency benchmark for the Kimi-Linear hybrid decode unit.
2	
3	Score = baseline_latency / solution_latency (speedup over the optimized-PyTorch
4	baseline.py), geomean over the context-length sweep. The solution is timed
5	first; a final next-token check against the reference makes a fast-but-wrong
6	solution score zero. Absolute tok/s at the longest context is the shippable
7	"single-GPU decode" number.
8	
9	Reported in the peak_fraction field as a speedup multiple (>1 means faster than
10	the baseline), not a [0,1] roofline fraction.
11	"""
12	from __future__ import annotations
13	
14	import sys
15	import time
16	from math import exp, log
17	from pathlib import Path
18	
19	import torch
20	import yaml
21	
22	
23	def _run(model, cfg, ctx, steps, seed, ref):
24	    h = ref.init_token(cfg, seed)
25	    st = ref.init_state(cfg, ctx, seed)
26	    with torch.no_grad():
27	        for _ in range(steps):
28	            h, st = model.step(h, st)
29	    torch.cuda.synchronize()
30	    return h
31	
32	
33	def _time(model, cfg, ctx, steps, seed, ref):
34	    _run(model, cfg, ctx, min(3, steps), seed, ref)   # warmup
35	    torch.cuda.synchronize()
36	    best = float("inf")
37	    for _ in range(int(yaml.safe_load(Path("problem.yaml").read_text()).get("num_perf_trials", 3))):
38	        t0 = time.perf_counter()
39	        h = _run(model, cfg, ctx, steps, seed, ref)
40	        best = min(best, time.perf_counter() - t0)
41	    return best, h
42

45	    impor

#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail
name="$1"
real="$2"
shift 2
if [ -z "$real" ]; then
    echo "$name is unavailable" >&2
    exit 127
fi
real_abs="$(readlink -f "$real" 2>/dev/null || printf '%s' "$real")"
case "$name" in
    uv)
        fallback="${REAL_UV_FALLBACK:-}"
        ;;
    python|python3)
        fallback="${REAL_PYTHON_FALLBACK:-}"
        ;;
    *)
        fallback=""
        ;;
esac
if [ -n "${RUN_DIR:-}" ] && [[ "$real_abs" == "${RUN_DIR}/bin/"* ]] && [ -n "$fallback" ]; then
    real="$fallback"
fi
if [ "${KBH_GPU_LOCK_HELD:-0}" = "1" ]; then
    exec "$real" "$@"
fi
if [ "${KBH_AGENT_PHASE:-0}" = "1" ]; then
    case "$name" in
        uv|python|python3|nvidia-smi|nvcc)
            exec "$real" "$@"
            ;;
        ncu|nsys)
            echo "$name is disabled during KernelBench parallel agent phase; official benchmarking runs under the GPU lock after generation." >&2
            exit 125
            ;;
    esac
fi
owner_file="${KBH_GPU_LOCK}.owner"
if [ -f "$owner_file" ]; then
    IFS=$'\t' read -r owner_pid owner_run_dir < "$owner_file" || true
    if [ "${owner_run_dir:-}" = "${RUN_DIR:-}" ] && kill -0 "${owner_pid:-}" 2>/dev/null; then
        exec "$real" "$@"
    fi
fi
{
    printf '%s wait pid=%s cmd=%s args=%q\n' "$(date -Is)" "$$" "$name" "$*" >&3
    lock_wait_timeout="${KBH_GPU_LOCK_WAIT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS:-}"
    if [ -

import time, torch
import reference as R
import baseline as B

dev = torch.device("cuda:0")
def run(model, cfg, ctx, steps, seed=7):
    h = R.init_token(cfg, seed); st = R.init_state(cfg, ctx, seed)
    with torch.no_grad():
        for _ in range(steps):
            h, st = model.step(h, st)
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); return h

for ctx, steps in [(2048,32),(8192,16),(16384,16)]:
    cfg = R.build_config({"n_experts":64})
    bm = B.Model(cfg).to(dev).eval()
    rm = R.Model(cfg).to(dev).eval()
    bm.load_state_dict(rm.state_dict(), strict=True)
    run(bm,cfg,ctx,3)  # warmup
    best=1e9
    for _ in range(3):
        t0=time.perf_counter(); run(bm,cfg,ctx,steps); best=min(best,time.perf_counter()-t0)
    print(f"baseline ctx={ctx}: {best*1e3/steps:.3f} ms/tok  ({steps/best:.1f} tok/s)")

+"""Standalone dev/test of the fused int4 dequant-GEMV Triton kernel."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+import reference as R
+
+GROUP = 128
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _gemv_w4a16_kernel(
+    x_ptr, wq_ptr, s_ptr, z_ptr, idx_ptr, y_ptr,
+    K, N, NG,
+    stride_xe, stride_xk,
+    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
+    stride_se, stride_sg, stride_sn,
+    stride_ye, stride_yn,
+    GROUP: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, USE_IDX: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_e = tl.program_id(1)
+    if USE_IDX:
+        e = tl.load(idx_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
+    else:
+        e = pid_e
+    n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    nmask = n < N
+    wq_e = wq_ptr + e * stride_we
+    s_e = s_ptr + e * stride_se
+    z_e = z_ptr + e * stride_se
+    x_e = x_ptr + pid_e * stride_xe
+    acc = tl.zeros([BLOCK_N], dtype=tl.float32)
+    HG = GROUP // 2  # packed rows per group
+    rows = tl.arange(0, HG)
+    for g in range(0, NG):
+        kp = g * HG + rows                       # [HG] packed-row indices
+        wq = tl.load(wq_e + kp[:, None] * stride_wk + n[None, :] * stride_wn,
+                     mask=nmask[None, :], other=0)
+        lo = (wq & 0xF).to(tl.float32)
+        hi = ((wq >> 4) & 0xF).to(tl.float32)
+        xe_ = tl.load(x_e + (2 * kp) * stride_xk)
+        xo_ = tl.load(x_e + (2 * kp + 1) * stride_xk)
+        raw = tl.sum(xe_[:, None] * lo + xo_[:, None] * hi, axis=0)   # [BLOCK_N]
+        xs = tl.sum(xe_ + xo_)                                        # scalar
+        s = tl.load(s_e + g * stride_sg + n * stride_sn, mask=nmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        z = tl.load(z_e + g * stride_sg + n * stride_sn, mask=nmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc += s * (raw - z * xs)
+    tl.store(y_ptr + pid_e * stride_ye + n * stride_yn, acc, mask=nmask)
+
+
+def gemv(x, wq, scales, zeros, idx=None, out=None, BLOCK_N=128):
+    """x:[K] or [E,K] fp32 ; wq:[E,Kp,N] uint8 ; scales/zeros:[E,NG,N] bf16.
+    idx:[Eact] int32 gather (or None -> e=slot). Returns [Eact,N] fp32."""
+    assert wq.dim() == 3
+    E, Kp, N = wq.shape
+    K = Kp * 2
+    NG = scales.shape[1]
+    if idx is not None:
+        Eact = idx.numel()
+        use_idx = True
+    else:
+        Eact = E
+        use_idx = False
+    if x.dim() == 1:
+        stride_xe, stride_xk = 0, x.stride(0)
+    else:
+        stride_xe, stride_xk = x.stride(0), x.stride(1)
+    if out is None:
+        out = torch.empty((Eact, N), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+    grid = (triton.cdiv(N, BLOCK_N), Eact)
+    _gemv_w4a16_kernel[grid](
+        x, wq, scales, zeros, idx if use_idx else x, out,
+        K, N, NG,
+        stride_xe, stride_xk,
+        wq.stride(0), wq.stride(1), wq.stride(2),
+        scales.stride(0), scales.stride(1), scales.stride(2),
+        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
+        GROUP=GROUP, BLOCK_N=BLOCK_N, USE_IDX=use_idx,
+    )
+    return out
+
+
+def _cos(a, b):
+    import torch.nn.functional as F
+    return F.cosine_similarity(a.float().flatten(), b.float().flatten(), dim=0).item()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    dev = "cuda"
+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    # Test single QuantLinear-style: in=2304, out=4096
+    for (K, N) in [(2304, 4096), (4096, 2304), (1024, 2304), (512, 8192), (2304, 576)]:
+        ql = R.QuantLinear(K, N).to(dev)
+        g = torch.Generator(device="cpu").manual_seed(42)
+        ql.init_random(g)
+        x = torch.randn(K, device=dev, dtype=torch.float32)
+        w = ql.weight_bf().float()                 # [K,N]
+        y_ref = x @ w
+        wq3 = ql.w_q.unsqueeze(0)
+        s3 = ql.scales.unsqueeze(0)
+        z3 = ql.zeros.unsqueeze(0)
+        y = gemv(x, wq3, s3, z3).squeeze(0)
+        print(f"K={K} N={N}: cos={_cos(y, y_ref):.6f}  maxabs={(y-y_ref).abs().max():.4e}  ymax={y_ref.abs().max():.2f}")
+
+    # Test batched experts with gather: E=64, in=2304, out=1024, pick 8
+    qe = R.QuantExperts(64, 2304, 1024).to(dev)
+    g = torch.Generator(device="cpu").manual_seed(7)
+    qe.init_random(g)
+    x = torch.randn(2304, device=dev, dtype=torch.float32)
+    idx = torch.tensor([3, 17, 40, 1, 63, 22, 9, 55], device=dev, dtype=torch.int32)
+    y = gemv(x, qe.w_q, qe.scales, qe.zeros, idx=idx)   # [8,1024]
+    for j, e in enumerate(idx.tolist()):
+        w = qe.weight_bf(e).float()
+        yref = x @ w
+        print(f"expert slot {j} (e={e}): cos={_cos(y[j], yref):.6f}")
+
+    # Test per-expert x (down-proj style): x [8,1024], gather
+    qe2 = R.QuantExperts(64, 1024, 2304).to(dev)
+    g = torch.Generator(device="cpu").manual_seed(11)
+    qe2.init_random(g)
+    xb = torch.randn(8, 1024, device=dev, dtype=torch.float32)
+    y2 = gemv(xb, qe2.w_q, qe2.scales, qe2.zeros, idx=idx)
+    for j, e in enumerate(idx.tolist()):
+        w = qe2.weight_bf(e).float()
+        yref = xb[j] @ w
+        print(f"down slot {j} (e={e}): cos={_cos(y2[j], yref):.6f}")

import torch, triton
import reference as R
from dev_gemv import gemv, _gemv_w4a16_kernel, GROUP
import triton.language as tl

dev="cuda"
def bench(fn, iters=200):
    for _ in range(20): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    import time; t0=time.perf_counter()
    for _ in range(iters): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    return (time.perf_counter()-t0)/iters*1e6  # us

# Single GEMVs at various shapes, tune BLOCK_N
for (K,N,name) in [(2304,4096,"kda_qkvg"),(4096,2304,"kda_o"),(2304,6144,"mla_q"),(512,8192,"mla_kvb"),(1024,2304,"moe_down")]:
    ql=R.QuantLinear(K,N).to(dev); g=torch.Generator(device="cpu").manual_seed(1); ql.init_random(g)
    x=torch.randn(K,device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
    wq3,s3,z3=ql.w_q[None],ql.scales[None],ql.zeros[None]
    wbytes=K*N*0.5/1e6
    best=None
    for BN in [64,128,256,512]:
        t=bench(lambda BN=BN: gemv(x,wq3,s3,z3,BLOCK_N=BN))
        bw=wbytes/t*1e6/1e3  # GB/s = MB/us *1e3... MB/us = GB/ms = TB/s*... let's do MB/(us)=> *1e6us/s /1e6MB/TB => TB/s = wbytes(MB)/t(us)
        tbs=wbytes/t  # MB/us = GB/ms = TB/s
        if best is None or t<best[1]: best=(BN,t,tbs)
    print(f"{name} K={K} N={N} ({wbytes:.2f}MB): best BLOCK_N={best[0]} {best[1]:.2f}us {best[2]:.2f}TB/s")

# Baseline dequant+matmul for comparison (kda_qkvg)
ql=R.QuantLinear(2304,4096).to(dev); g=torch.Generator(device="cpu").manual_seed(1); ql.init_random(g)
x=torch.randn(2304,device=dev,dtype=torch.bfloat16)
def base():
    w=ql.weight_bf(); return x@w
print(f"baseline dequant+matmul kda_qkvg: {bench(base):.2f}us")

# Batched MoE gate: E=8 gather, in=2304 out=1024
qe=R.QuantExperts(64,2304,1024).to(dev); g=torch.Generator(device="cpu").manual_seed(2); qe.init_random(g)
xx=torch.randn(2304,device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
idx=torch.tensor([3,17,40,1,63,22,9,55],device=dev,dtype=torch.int32)
wbytes=8*2304*1024*0.5/1e6
for BN in [64,128,256]:
    t=bench(lambda BN=BN: gemv(xx,qe.w_q,qe.scales,qe.zeros,idx=idx,BLOCK_N=BN))
    print(f"moe_gate x8 ({wbytes:.2f}MB): BLOCK_N={BN} {t:.2f}us {wbytes/t:.2f}TB/s")
EOF

import torch, time
import reference as R
from dev_gemv import gemv

dev="cuda"
def bench(fn, iters=300):
    for _ in range(30): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); t0=time.perf_counter()
    for _ in range(iters): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); return (time.perf_counter()-t0)/iters*1e6

shapes=[(2304,4096,"kda_qkvg"),(4096,2304,"kda_o"),(2304,6144,"mla_q"),(512,8192,"mla_kvb"),(1024,2304,"down1")]
for (K,N,name) in shapes:
    ql=R.QuantLinear(K,N).to(dev); g=torch.Generator(device="cpu").manual_seed(1); ql.init_random(g)
    x=torch.randn(K,device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
    wq3,s3,z3=ql.w_q[None],ql.scales[None],ql.zeros[None]
    wb=K*N*0.5/1e6
    best=(None,1e9,0)
    for BN in [32,64,128,256]:
        for SK in [1,2,4,8,16]:
            try:
                t=bench(lambda BN=BN,SK=SK: gemv(x,wq3,s3,z3,BLOCK_N=BN,SPLIT_K=SK))
            except Exception: continue
            if t<best[1]: best=(f"BN{BN}/SK{SK}",t,wb/t)
    print(f"{name:10s} K={K} N={N} ({wb:.2f}MB): {best[0]} {best[1]:.2f}us {best[2]:.2f}TB/s")

# Batched MoE: gate x8 (in2304,out1024) and down x8 (in1024,out2304)
for (Ein,Eout,name) in [(2304,1024,"moe_gate_x8"),(1024,2304,"moe_down_x8")]:

    idx=torch.tensor([3,17,40,1,63,22,9,55],device=dev,dtype=torch.int32)
    if name=="moe_gate_x8":
        x=torch.randn(Ein,device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
    else:
        x=torch.randn(8,Ein,device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
    wb=8*Ein*Eout*0.5/1e6
    best=(None,1e9,0)
    for BN in [32,64,128,256]:
        for SK in [1,2,4,8]:
            try:
                t=bench(lambda BN=BN,SK=SK: gemv(x,qe.w_q,qe.scales,qe.zeros,idx=idx,BLOCK_N=BN,SPLIT_K=SK))
            except Exception: continue
            if t<best[1]: best=(f"BN{BN}/SK{SK}",t,wb/t)
    print(f"{name:10s} ({wb:.2f}MB): {best[0]} {best[1]:.2f}us {best[2]:.2f}TB/s")

import torch, time
import reference as R
from dev_gemv import gemv

dev="cuda"
ql=R.QuantLinear(2304,4096).to(dev); g=torch.Generator(device="cpu").manual_seed(1); ql.init_random(g)
x=torch.randn(2304,device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
wq3,s3,z3=ql.w_q[None],ql.scales[None],ql.zeros[None]

def wall(fn,it=500):
    for _ in range(30): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); t0=time.perf_counter()
    for _ in range(it): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); return (time.perf_counter()-t0)/it*1e6
def gpu(fn,it=500):
    for _ in range(30): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    s=torch.cuda.Event(True); e=torch.cuda.Event(True)
    s.record()
    for _ in range(it): fn()
    e.record(); torch.cuda.synchronize()
    return s.elapsed_time(e)/it*1e3  # us

f=lambda: gemv(x,wq3,s3,z3,BLOCK_N=256,SPLIT_K=16)
print(f"gemv BN256/SK16: wall={wall(f):.2f}us gpu={gpu(f):.2f}us")
f1=lambda: gemv(x,wq3,s3,z3,BLOCK_N=64,SPLIT_K=1)
print(f"gemv BN64/SK1:   wall={wall(f1):.2f}us gpu={gpu(f1):.2f}us")

# launch overhead: trivial torch op
y=torch.empty(4096,device=dev)
f2=lambda: y.add_(1.0)
print(f"add_ :           wall={wall(f2):.2f}us gpu={gpu(f2):.2f}us")

# Try CUDA graph capture of a single gemv
out=torch.empty((1,4096),device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
gemv(x,wq3,s3,z3,out=out,BLOCK_N=256,SPLIT_K=16)  # warm
torch.cuda.synchronize()
gph=torch.cuda.CUDAGraph()
s=torch.cuda.Stream(); s.wait_stream(torch.cuda.current_stream())
with torch.cuda.stream(s):
    for _ in range(3): gemv(x,wq3,s3,z3,out=out,BLOCK_N=256,SPLIT_K=16)
torch.cuda.current_stream().wait_stream(s)
with torch.cuda.graph(gph):
    gemv(x,wq3,s3,z3,out=out,BLOCK_N=256,SPLIT_K=16)
print(f"graphed gemv:    wall={wall(lambda: gph.replay()):.2f}us")
EOF

+++ b//home/shadeform/mega/outputs/runs/20260618_170335_claude_claude-opus-4-8_03_kimi_linear_decode/repo/problems/03_kimi_linear_decode/solution.py

+"""Fused W4A16 Kimi-Linear hybrid decode (batch=1).
+
+Beats baseline.py by fusing the int4 unpack + per-group asymmetric dequant
+directly into the GEMV (the weights are streamed once as int4, never
+materialized to bf16), plus the MLA absorb reformulation so the latent KV cache
+is never re-expanded through kv_b.
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import torch
+import torch.nn as nn
+import torch.nn.functional as F
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+EPS = 1.0e-6
+GROUP = 128
+
+
+# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
+# Fused int4 dequant GEMV (batch=1), split-K, optional expert gather.
+# y[e,n] = sum_k x[e_or_0,k] * (unpack(wq)[e,k,n] - zeros[e,k//G,n]) * scales[..]
+# Using the group identity:
+#   y = sum_g scales_g * ( sum_{k in g} x_k*w_k  -  zeros_g * sum_{k in g} x_k )
+# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
+@triton.jit
+def _gemv_kernel(
+    x_ptr, wq_ptr, s_ptr, z_ptr, idx_ptr, y_ptr,
+    K, N, NG,
+    stride_xe, stride_xk,
+    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
+    stride_se, stride_sg, stride_sn,
+    stride_ye, stride_yn,
+    GROUP: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, USE_IDX: tl.constexpr,
+    SPLIT_K: tl.constexpr, GPER: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_e = tl.program_id(1)
+    pid_k = tl.program_id(2)
+    if USE_IDX:
+        e = tl.load(idx_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
+    else:
+        e = pid_e
+    n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    nmask = n < N
+    wq_e = wq_ptr + e * stride_we
+    s_e = s_ptr + e * stride_se
+    z_e = z_ptr + e * stride_se
+    x_e = x_ptr + pid_e * stride_xe
+    acc = tl.zeros([BLOCK_N], dtype=tl.float32)
+    HG: tl.constexpr = GROUP // 2
+    rows = tl.arange(0, HG)
+    for gg in range(0, GPER):
+        g = pid_k * GPER + gg
+        if g < NG:
+            kp = g * HG + rows
+            wq = tl.load(wq_e + kp[:, None] * stride_wk + n[None, :] * stride_wn,
+                         mask=nmask[None, :], other=0)
+            lo = (wq & 0xF).to(tl.float32)
+            hi = ((wq >> 4) & 0xF).to(tl.float32)
+            xe_ = tl.load(x_e + (2 * kp) * stride_xk)
+            xo_ = tl.load(x_e + (2 * kp + 1) * stride_xk)
+            raw = tl.sum(xe_[:, None] * lo + xo_[:, None] * hi, axis=0)
+            xs = tl.sum(xe_ + xo_)
+            s = tl.load(s_e + g * stride_sg + n * stride_sn, mask=nmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+            z = tl.load(z_e + g * stride_sg + n * stride_sn, mask=nmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+            acc += s * (raw - z * xs)
+    if SPLIT_K == 1:
+        tl.store(y_ptr + pid_e * stride_ye + n * stride_yn, acc, mask=nmask)
+    else:
+        tl.atomic_add(y_ptr + pid_e * stride_ye + n * stride_yn, acc, mask=nmask)
+
+
+def gemv(x, wq, scales, zeros, idx=None, out=None, BLOCK_N=128, SPLIT_K=8):
+    """x:[K] (shared) or [Eact,K]; wq:[E,K//2,N]; s/z:[E,NG,N]; -> [Eact,N] fp32."""
+    E, Kp, N = wq.shape
+    K = Kp * 2
+    NG = scales.shape[1]
+    use_idx = idx is not None
+    Eact = idx.numel() if use_idx else E
+    if x.dim() == 1:
+        stride_xe, stride_xk = 0, x.stride(0)
+    else:
+        stride_xe, stride_xk = x.stride(0), x.stride(1)
+    SPLIT_K = min(SPLIT_K, NG)
+    GPER = (NG + SPLIT_K - 1) // SPLIT_K
+    if out is None:
+        out = torch.empty((Eact, N), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+    if SPLIT_K > 1:
+        out.zero_()
+    grid = (triton.cdiv(N, BLOCK_N), Eact, SPLIT_K)
+    _gemv_kernel[grid](
+        x, wq, scales, zeros, idx if use_idx else x, out,
+        K, N, NG,
+        stride_xe, stride_xk,
+        wq.stride(0), wq.stride(1), wq.stride(2),
+        scales.stride(0), scales.stride(1), scales.stride(2),
+        out.stride(0), out.stride(1),
+        GROUP=GROUP, BLOCK_N=BLOCK_N, USE_IDX=use_idx, SPLIT_K=SPLIT_K, GPER=GPER,
+    )
+    return out
+
+
+def _unpack_dequant(wq, scales, zeros, group=GROUP):
+    """Dequant a single [K//2,N] int4 weight to [K,N] bf16 (only used for kv_b)."""
+    Kp, N = wq.shape
+    wu = torch.empty((2 * Kp, N), dtype=torch.uint8, device=wq.device)
+    wu[0::2] = wq & 0xF
+    wu[1::2] = (wq >> 4) & 0xF
+    s = scales.repeat_interleave(group, dim=0)
+    z = zeros.repeat_interleave(group, dim=0)
+    return (wu.to(torch.bfloat16) - z) * s
+
+
+# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
+# modules (buffer/param names identical to reference for state_dict load)
+# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #
+class QuantLinear(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(self, in_f, out_f, group=GROUP):
+        super().__init__()
+        self.in_f, self.out_f, self.group = in_f, out_f, group
+        ng = in_f // group
+        self.register_buffer("w_q", torch.zeros(in_f // 2, out_f, dtype=torch.uint8))
+        self.register_buffer("scales", torch.zeros(ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
+        self.register_buffer("zeros", torch.zeros(ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
+
+
+class QuantExperts(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(self, n, in_f, out_f, group=GROUP):
+        super().__init__()
+        self.n, self.in_f, self.out_f, self.group = n, in_f, out_f, group
+        ng = in_f // group
+        self.register_buffer("w_q", torch.zeros(n, in_f // 2, out_f, dtype=torch.uint8))
+        self.register_buffer("scales", torch.zeros(n, ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
+        self.register_buffer("zeros", torch.zeros(n, ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
+
+
+def _rmsnorm(x, w):
+    xf = x.float()
+    xf = xf * torch.rsqrt(xf.pow(2).mean(-1, keepdim=True) + EPS)
+    return (xf * w.float()).to(x.dtype)
+
+
+def _rope_cossin(pos, dim, theta, device):
+    inv = 1.0 / (theta ** (torch.arange(0, dim, 2, device=device, dtype=torch.float32) / dim)

... (7483 more chars)

import torch, time
import reference as R
import solution as S

dev="cuda"
cfg=R.build_config({"n_experts":64})
sm=S.Model(cfg).to(dev).eval()
rm=R.Model(cfg).to(dev).eval()
sm.load_state_dict(rm.state_dict(),strict=True)

def wall(fn,it):
    for _ in range(5): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); t0=time.perf_counter()
    for _ in range(it): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); return (time.perf_counter()-t0)/it*1e6
def gpu(fn,it):
    for _ in range(5): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    s=torch.cuda.Event(True); e=torch.cuda.Event(True); s.record()
    for _ in range(it): fn()
    e.record(); torch.cuda.synchronize(); return s.elapsed_time(e)/it*1e3

for ctx in [2048, 16384]:
    st=R.init_state(cfg,ctx,7); h=R.init_token(cfg,7)
    def step():
        global h,st
        h,st=sm.step(h,st)
    # need fresh state each measure since cache grows; measure single step from fixed state
    def one():
        st2=R.init_state(cfg,ctx,7); hh=R.init_token(cfg,7)
        with torch.no_grad(): o,_=sm.step(hh,st2)
        return o
    print(f"ctx={ctx}: full step wall={wall(one,30):.1f}us gpu={gpu(one,30):.1f}us")

# per-block-type single step cost (ctx=16384)
ctx=16384
with torch.no_grad():
    # KDA block 0
    st=R.init_state(cfg,ctx,7); h=R.init_token(cfg,7)
    blkK=sm.blocks[0]; blkM=sm.blocks[3]
    def kda():
        x=h; stt=R.init_state(cfg,ctx,7)[0]
        return blkK.step(x, stt)
    def mla():
        x=h; stt=R.init_state(cfg,ctx,7)[3]
        return blkM.step(x, stt)
    print(f"KDA block wall={wall(kda,30):.1f}us gpu={gpu(kda,30):.1f}us")
    print(f"MLA block wall={wall(mla,30):.1f}us gpu={gpu(mla,30):.1f}us")
    # just attn vs moe
    import torch.nn.functional as F
    def kda_attn():
        stt=R.init_state(cfg,ctx,7)[0]; return blkK.attn.step(S._rmsnorm(h,blkK.attn_norm), stt)
    def moe():
        return blkK.moe.step(S._rmsnorm(h,blkK.moe_norm))
    def mla_attn():
        stt=R.init_state(cfg,ctx,7)[3]; return blkM.attn.step(S._rmsnorm(h,blkM.attn_norm), stt)
    print(f"  KDA.attn wall={wall(kda_attn,50):.1f}us gpu={gpu(kda_attn,50):.1f}us")
    print(f"  MoE      wall={wall(moe,50):.1f}us gpu={gpu(moe,50):.1f}us")
    print(f"  MLA.attn wall={wall(mla_attn,50):.1f}us gpu={gpu(mla_attn,50):.1f}us")

import torch, time
import reference as R
import solution as S

dev="cuda"
cfg=R.build_config({"n_experts":64})
sm=S.Model(cfg).to(dev).eval()
rm=R.Model(cfg).to(dev).eval()

    s=torch.cuda.Event(True); e=torch.cuda.Event(True); s.record()

+"""Dev/test the fused KDA gated-delta recurrence kernel."""
+import torch, time
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+import torch.nn.functional as F
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _kda_recur_kernel(
+    S_ptr, q_ptr, k_ptr, v_ptr, g_ptr, beta_ptr, o_ptr,
+    stride_sh, stride_sk, stride_sv,
+    DK: tl.constexpr, DV: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_V: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    pid_h = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_v = tl.program_id(1)
+    koff = tl.arange(0, DK)
+    voff = pid_v * BLOCK_V + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_V)
+    key = tl.load(k_ptr + pid_h * DK + koff)
+    qry = tl.load(q_ptr + pid_h * DK + koff)
+    gg = tl.load(g_ptr + pid_h * DK + koff)
+    beta = tl.load(beta_ptr + pid_h)
+    val = tl.load(v_ptr + pid_h * DV + voff)
+    sbase = S_ptr + pid_h * stride_sh + koff[:, None] * stride_sk + voff[None, :] * stride_sv
+    S = tl.load(sbase)                                   # [DK, BLOCK_V]
+    eg = tl.exp(gg)                                      # [DK]
+    Sd = S * eg[:, None]
+    pred = tl.sum(Sd * key[:, None], axis=0)            # [BLOCK_V]
+    delta = val - pred
+    Snew = Sd + (beta * key)[:, None] * delta[None, :]  # [DK, BLOCK_V]
+    o = tl.sum(Snew * qry[:, None], axis=0)             # [BLOCK_V]
+    tl.store(sbase, Snew)
+    tl.store(o_ptr + pid_h * DV + voff, o)
+
+
+def kda_recur(S, q, k, v, g, beta, BLOCK_V=32):
+    """S:[H,DK,DV] fp32 (updated in place); q,k,v,g:[H,DK] fp32; beta:[H] fp32.
+    Returns o:[H,DV] fp32."""
+    H, DK, DV = S.shape
+    o = torch.empty((H, DV), device=S.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+    grid = (H, triton.cdiv(DV, BLOCK_V))
+    _kda_recur_kernel[grid](
+        S, q, k, v, g, beta, o,
+        S.stride(0), S.stride(1), S.stride(2),
+        DK=DK, DV=DV, BLOCK_V=BLOCK_V,
+    )
+    return o
+
+
+def ref_recur(S, q, k, v, g, beta):
+    S = S * g.exp()[:, :, None]
+    pred = (S * k[:, :, None]).sum(1)
+    S = S + beta[:, None, None] * k[:, :, None] * (v - pred)[:, None, :]
+    o = (S * q[:, :, None]).sum(1)
+    return S, o
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    dev = "cuda"
+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    H, DK, DV = 32, 128, 128
+    for trial in range(3):
+        S0 = torch.randn(H, DK, DV, device=dev) * 0.05
+        q = torch.randn(H, DK, device=dev) * 0.1
+        k = torch.randn(H, DK, device=dev) * 0.1
+        v = torch.randn(H, DK, device=dev) * 0.1
+        g = -F.softplus(torch.randn(H, DK, device=dev))
+        beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(H, device=dev))
+        S_ref, o_ref = ref_recur(S0.clone(), q, k, v, g, beta)
+        S_t = S0.clone()
+        o_t = kda_recur(S_t, q, k, v, g, beta)
+        co = F.cosine_similarity(o_ref.flatten(), o_t.flatten(), dim=0).item()
+        cs = F.cosine_similarity(S_ref.flatten(), S_t.flatten(), dim=0).item()
+        print(f"trial {trial}: o cos={co:.6f}  S cos={cs:.6f}  o_err={(o_ref-o_t).abs().max():.2e}  S_err={(S_ref-S_t).abs().max():.2e}")
+
+    # bench
+    def gpu(fn, it=200):
+        for _ in range(20): fn()
+        torch.cuda.synchronize(); s=torch.cuda.Event(True); e=torch.cuda.Event(True); s.record()
+        for _ in range(it): fn()
+        e.record(); torch.cuda.synchronize(); return s.elapsed_time(e)/it*1e3
+    S_t = S0.clone()
+    for bv in [16, 32, 64, 128]:
+        print(f"BLOCK_V={bv}: {gpu(lambda bv=bv: kda_recur(S_t.clone(), q,k,v,g,beta, BLOCK_V=bv)):.2f}us")
+    print(f"torch recur: {gpu(lambda: ref_recur(S0.clone(), q,k,v,g,beta)):.2f}us")
args

import torch, time
import reference as R
from solution import gemv

for _ in range(30):

        gemv(x, ql.w_q, ql.scales, ql.zeros, out=out, BLOCK_N=256, SPLIT_K=16)

def wall(fn,it=100):
    for _ in range(10): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); t0=time.perf_counter()
    for _ in range(it): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); return (time.perf_counter()-t0)/it*1e6

s=torch.cuda.Stream(); s.wait_stream(torch.cuda.current_stream())
with torch.cuda.stream(s):
    for _ in range(3): run()
torch.cuda.current_stream().wait_stream(s)
gph=torch.cuda.CUDAGraph()
with torch.cuda.graph(gph):
    run()
print(f"graphed 30 gemv: {wall(lambda: gph.replay()):.1f}us  ({wall(lambda: gph.replay())/30:.2f}us/gemv)")

def run1():
    for ql,x,out in mods:
        gemv(x, ql.w_q, ql.scales, ql.zeros, out=out, BLOCK_N=64, SPLIT_K=1)
print(f"eager 30 gemv SK1: {wall(run1):.1f}us")
run1(); torch.cuda.synchronize()
s=torch.cuda.Stream(); s.wait_stream(torch.cuda.current_stream())

cat > dev_bw.py << 'EOF'
import torch, triton, triton.language as tl
import reference as R

dev="cuda"
def gpu(fn,it=300):
    for _ in range(30): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); s=torch.cuda.Event(True); e=torch.cuda.Event(True); s.record()
    for _ in range(it): fn()
    e.record(); torch.cuda.synchronize(); return s.elapsed_time(e)/it*1e3

# pure read bandwidth of a [Kp,N] uint8 tensor
@triton.jit
def _read(wq_ptr, out_ptr, Kp, N, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
    pid_n=tl.program_id(0); pid_k=tl.program_id(1)
    n=pid_n*BLOCK_N+tl.arange(0,BLOCK_N)
    acc=tl.zeros([BLOCK_N],dtype=tl.float32)
    for k0 in range(0, Kp, BLOCK_K):
        kk=k0+pid_k*0+tl.arange(0,BLOCK_K)
        w=tl.load(wq_ptr+kk[:,None]*N+n[None,:], mask=(kk[:,None]<Kp)&(n[None,:]<N), other=0)
        acc+=tl.sum(w.to(tl.float32),axis=0)
    tl.atomic_add(out_ptr+n, acc, mask=n<N)

ql=R.QuantLinear(2304,4096).to(dev); g=torch.Generator(device="cpu").manual_seed(1); ql.init_random(g)
wq=ql.w_q  # [1152,4096]
Kp,N=wq.shape
MB=Kp*N/1e6
out=torch.zeros(N,device=dev)
def read(BN,BK):
    out.zero_()
    grid=(triton.cdiv(N,BN),1)
    _read[grid](wq,out,Kp,N,BLOCK_N=BN,BLOCK_K=BK)
for BN in [128,256,512,1024]:
    t=gpu(lambda BN=BN: read(BN,Kp))

import torch, triton, triton.language as tl
import reference as R

dev="cuda"
def gpu(fn,it=300):
    for _ in range(30): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); s=torch.cuda.Event(True); e=torch.cuda.Event(True); s.record()
    for _ in range(it): fn()
    e.record(); torch.cuda.synchronize(); return s.elapsed_time(e)/it*1e3

@triton.jit
def _read(wq_ptr, out_ptr, Kp, N, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr, NK: tl.constexpr):
    pid_n=tl.program_id(0)
    n=pid_n*BLOCK_N+tl.arange(0,BLOCK_N)
    acc=tl.zeros([BLOCK_N],dtype=tl.float32)
    for k0 in range(0, NK):
        kk=k0*BLOCK_K+tl.arange(0,BLOCK_K)
        w=tl.load(wq_ptr+kk[:,None]*N+n[None,:], mask=(kk[:,None]<Kp)&(n[None,:]<N), other=0)
        acc+=tl.sum(w.to(tl.float32),axis=0)
    tl.store(out_ptr+n, acc, mask=n<N)

ql=R.QuantLinear(2304,4096).to(dev); g=torch.Generator(device="cpu").manual_seed(1); ql.init_random(g)
wq=ql.w_q; Kp,N=wq.shape; MB=Kp*N/1e6
out=torch.zeros(N,device=dev)
def read(BN,BK):
    grid=(triton.cdiv(N,BN),); NK=triton.cdiv(Kp,BK)
    _read[grid](wq,out,Kp,N,BLOCK_N=BN,BLOCK_K=BK,NK=NK)
for BN in [64,128,256]:
    for BK in [64,128,256]:
        t=gpu(lambda BN=BN,BK=BK: read(BN,BK))

import torch, triton, triton.language as tl
dev="cuda"
def gpu(fn,it=100):
    for _ in range(20): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); s=torch.cuda.Event(True); e=torch.cuda.Event(True); s.record()
    for _ in range(it): fn()
    e.record(); torch.cuda.synchronize(); return s.elapsed_time(e)/it*1e3

for MB in [10,50,100,400]:
    n=int(MB*1e6//4)
    a=torch.randn(n,device=dev); b=torch.randn(n,device=dev); c=torch.empty(n,device=dev)
    # copy_: read 4*n, write 4*n
    t=gpu(lambda: c.copy_(a)); print(f"copy {MB}MB: {t:.1f}us  {2*MB/t:.2f}TB/s")
    # add: read 2x, write 1x
    t=gpu(lambda: torch.add(a,b,out=c)); print(f"add  {MB}MB: {t:.1f}us  {3*MB/t:.2f}TB/s")
    # sum: read 1x
    t=gpu(lambda: torch.sum(a)); print(f"sum  {MB}MB: {t:.1f}us  {MB/t:.2f}TB/s")

# triton pure read-reduce of big uint8
@triton.jit
def _rd(p, o, n, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
    pid=tl.program_id(0); off=pid*BLOCK+tl.arange(0,BLOCK)
    x=tl.load(p+off, mask=off<n, other=0)
    s=tl.sum(x.to(tl.float32))
    tl.atomic_add(o, s)
for MB in [50,200]:
    n=int(MB*1e6); p=torch.randint(0,255,(n,),device=dev,dtype=torch.uint8); o=torch.zeros(1,device=dev)
    def rd():
        o.zero_(); _rd[(triton.cdiv(n,1024),)](p,o,n,BLOCK=1024)
    t=gpu(rd); print(f"triton read {MB}MB: {t:.1f}us  {MB/t:.2f}TB/s")

import torch, triton, triton.language as tl
import reference as R

dev="cuda"
def gpu(fn,it=300):
    for _ in range(30): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); s=torch.cuda.Event(True); e=torch.cuda.Event(True); s.record()
    for _ in range(it): fn()
    e.record(); torch.cuda.synchronize(); return s.elapsed_time(e)/it*1e3

# torch bf16 GEMV target: x[K] @ W[K,N]
K,N=2304,4096
Wbf=torch.randn(K,N,device=dev,dtype=torch.bfloat16)
xb=torch.randn(K,device=dev,dtype=torch.bfloat16)
MB_bf=K*N*2/1e6
t=gpu(lambda: xb@Wbf); print(f"torch bf16 GEMV [{K},{N}] ({MB_bf:.1f}MB bf16): {t:.2f}us {MB_bf/t:.2f}TB/s")
# torch bf16 batched E=4
Wbf4=torch.randn(4,K,N,device=dev,dtype=torch.bfloat16)
t=gpu(lambda: torch.einsum("k,ekn->en", xb, Wbf4)); print(f"torch bf16 E=4: {t:.2f}us {4*MB_bf/t:.2f}TB/s")

# Tunable kernel with num_warps/num_stages
@triton.jit
def _k(x_ptr,wq_ptr,s_ptr,z_ptr,y_ptr,K,N,NG,
       se,sg,sn, GROUP:tl.constexpr,BLOCK_N:tl.constexpr,SPLIT_K:tl.constexpr,GPER:tl.constexpr):
    pid_n=tl.program_id(0); pid_e=tl.program_id(1); pid_k=tl.program_id(2)
    n=pid_n*BLOCK_N+tl.arange(0,BLOCK_N); nmask=n<N
    wq_e=wq_ptr+pid_e*(K//2)*N; s_e=s_ptr+pid_e*se; z_e=z_ptr+pid_e*se
    acc=tl.zeros([BLOCK_N],dtype=tl.float32)
    HG:tl.constexpr=GROUP//2; rows=tl.arange(0,HG)
    for gg in range(0,GPER):
        g=pid_k*GPER+gg
        if g<NG:
            kp=g*HG+rows
            wq=tl.load(wq_e+kp[:,None]*N+n[None,:],mask=nmask[None,:],other=0)
            lo=(wq&0xF).to(tl.float32); hi=((wq>>4)&0xF).to(tl.float32)
            xe_=tl.load(x_ptr+2*kp); xo_=tl.load(x_ptr+2*kp+1)
            raw=tl.sum(xe_[:,None]*lo+xo_[:,None]*hi,axis=0); xs=tl.sum(xe_+xo_)
            s=tl.load(s_e+g*sg+n*sn,mask=nmask,other=0.).to(tl.float32)
            z=tl.load(z_e+g*sg+n*sn,mask=nmask,other=0.).to(tl.float32)
            acc+=s*(raw-z*xs)
    if SPLIT_K==1: tl.store(y_ptr+pid_e*N+n,acc,mask=nmask)
    else: tl.atomic_add(y_ptr+pid_e*N+n,acc,mask=nmask)

E=4
wq=torch.randint(0,255,(E,K//2,N),device=dev,dtype=torch.uint8)
sc=torch.randn(E,K//128,N,device=dev,dtype=torch.bfloat16).abs()*0.01
ze=torch.randint(0,15,(E,K//128,N),device=dev).to(torch.bfloat16)
x=torch.randn(K,device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
NG=K//128; MB=E*K*N*0.5/1e6
out=torch.empty((E,N),device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
def run(BN,SK,nw,ns):
    GPER=(NG+SK-1)//SK
    if SK>1: out.zero_()
    _k[(triton.cdiv(N,BN),E,SK)](x,wq,sc,ze,out,K,N,NG,sc.stride(0),sc.stride(1),sc.stride(2),
        GROUP=128,BLOCK_N=BN,SPLIT_K=SK,GPER=GPER,num_warps=nw,num_stages=ns)
best=(None,1e9)
for BN in [64,128,256]:
    for SK in [1,2,3,6,9,18]:
        for nw in [1,2,4,8]:
            for ns in [1,2,3,4]:
                try: t=gpu(lambda: run(BN,SK,nw,ns))
                except Exception: continue
                if t<best[1]: best=(f"BN{BN}/SK{SK}/nw{nw}/ns{ns}",t)
print(f"tuned kernel E=4 ({MB:.1f}MB): {best[0]} {best[1]:.2f}us {MB/best[1]:.2f}TB/s")

+@triton.jit
+def _kda_recur_kernel(
+    S_ptr, q_ptr, k_ptr, v_ptr, g_ptr, beta_ptr, o_ptr,
+    stride_sh, stride_sk, stride_sv,
+    DK: tl.constexpr, DV: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_V: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    pid_h = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_v = tl.program_id(1)
+    koff = tl.arange(0, DK)
+    voff = pid_v * BLOCK_V + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_V)
+    key = tl.load(k_ptr + pid_h * DK + koff)
+    qry = tl.load(q_ptr + pid_h * DK + koff)
+    gg = tl.load(g_ptr + pid_h * DK + koff)
+    beta = tl.load(beta_ptr + pid_h)
+    val = tl.load(v_ptr + pid_h * DV + voff)
+    sbase = S_ptr + pid_h * stride_sh + koff[:, None] * stride_sk + voff[None, :] * stride_sv
+    S = tl.load(sbase)
+    Sd = S * tl.exp(gg)[:, None]
+    pred = tl.sum(Sd * key[:, None], axis=0)
+    Snew = Sd + (beta * key)[:, None] * (val - pred)[None, :]
+    o = tl.sum(Snew * qry[:, None], axis=0)
+    tl.store(sbase, Snew)
+    tl.store(o_ptr + pid_h * DV + voff, o)
+
+
+def kda_recur(S, q, k, v, g, beta, BLOCK_V=64):
+    """S:[H,DK,DV] fp32 updated in place; q,k,v,g:[H,DK]; beta:[H]; -> o:[H,DV]."""
+    H, DK, DV = S.shape
+    o = torch.empty((H, DV), device=S.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+    grid = (H, triton.cdiv(DV, BLOCK_V))
+    _kda_recur_kernel[grid](
+        S, q, k, v, g, beta, o,
+        S.stride(0), S.stride(1), S.stride(2),
+        DK=DK, DV=DV, BLOCK_V=BLOCK_V,
+    )
+    return o

print("o vs sum(Sin*q):", F.cosine_similarity(o.flatten(),o_from_S.flatten(),dim=0).item())

print("q stride", q.stride(), "shape", q.shape)
# run twice
o2=S.kda_recur(st["S"].clone(), q,k,v,g,beta)
print("determinism o vs o2:", F.cosine_similarity(o.flatten(),o2.flatten(),dim=0).item())

Found it: the **autotune corruption bug**. With atomic-add kernels, Triton's autotuner benchmarks many configs writing to the same output buffer without re-zeroing, then the final launch atomic-adds onto that garbage. Triton has `reset_to_zero` for exactly this. Let me verify its behavior in this version.

The torch profiler reveals the real culprit: **MLA softmax over `dim=0` is 1.138 ms/step (47%!)** — reducing over the strided 16384-length outer dim hits PyTorch's slow "spatial softmax" path. Plus `_unpack_dequant` of kv_b runs every step (it's a constant weight). Let me rewrite MLA: precompute the kv_b dequant once, transpose scores to `[H, L]` so softmax is over the contiguous last dim, and use bf16 tensor-core matmuls over the cache.

+    def _conv_g(self, val, buf, idx):
+        # val:[C] fp32, buf:[3,C] bf16 (in-place ring shift), conv_w[idx]:[C,4]
+        w = self.conv_w[idx].float()
+        out = F.silu(buf[0].float() * w[:, 0] + buf[1].float() * w[:, 1]
+                     + buf[2].float() * w[:, 2] + val * w[:, 3])
+        buf[0].copy_(buf[1])
+        buf[1].copy_(buf[2])
+        buf[2].copy_(val.to(buf.dtype))
+        return out
+
+    def step_g(self, x, S_buf, cq, ck, cv):
+        H, Dk = self.cfg.kda_heads, self.cfg.kda_head_dim
+        if not hasattr(self, "_wq"):
+            self._stack()
+        xf = x.float()
+        qkvg = gemv(xf, self._wq, self._s, self._z)
+        q = self._conv_g(qkvg[0], cq, 0)
+        k = self._conv_g(qkvg[1], ck, 1)
+        v = self._conv_g(qkvg[2], cv, 2)
+        q = (q.view(H, Dk) * self.scale).contiguous()
+        k = k.view(H, Dk).contiguous()
+        v = v.view(H, Dk).contiguous()
+        g = (-F.softplus(qkvg[3].float())).view(H, Dk).contiguous()
+        beta = torch.sigmoid(self.beta_proj(x).float()).contiguous()
+        o = kda_recur(S_buf, q, k, v, g, beta)
+        of = o.reshape(H * Dk)
+        return gemv(of, self.o_proj.w_q, self.o_proj.scales, self.o_proj.zeros).squeeze(0).to(torch.bfloat16)

         of = o.reshape(H * vh).float()

+    def step_g(self, x, c_kv_buf, k_rope_buf, pos, maxlen):
+        """Graph variant: pos is a [1] int64 GPU scalar; cache written in place at pos."""
+        cfg = self.cfg
+        H = cfg.mla_heads
+        nope, rope, vh, lora = cfg.qk_nope, cfg.qk_rope, cfg.v_head, cfg.kv_lora
+        if not hasattr(self, "_Wkn"):
+            self._prep()
+        xf = x.float()
+        q = gemv(xf, self.q_proj.w_q, self.q_proj.scales, self.q_proj.zeros).squeeze(0).view(H, nope + rope)
+        q_nope = q[:, :nope]
+        q_rope = q[:, nope:]
+        kv = gemv(xf, self.kv_a.w_q, self.kv_a.scales, self.kv_a.zeros).squeeze(0)
+        c_kv_new = kv[:lora].to(torch.bfloat16)
+        k_rope_new = kv[lora:]
+        inv = self._inv
+        ang = pos.float() * inv                                  # [rope/2]
+        cos, sin = torch.cos(ang), torch.sin(ang)
+        q_rope = _apply_rope(q_rope, cos, sin).to(torch.bfloat16)
+        k_rope_new = _apply_rope(k_rope_new, cos, sin).to(torch.bfloat16)
+        c_kv_buf.index_copy_(0, pos, c_kv_new[None])
+        k_rope_buf.index_copy_(0, pos, k_rope_new[None])
+        q_absorb = torch.einsum("hdc,hc->hd", self._Wkn, q_nope.to(torch.bfloat16))    # [H,512]
+        scores = (q_absorb @ c_kv_buf.t() + q_rope @ k_rope_buf.t()).float() * self.scale  # [H,maxlen]
+        mask = torch.arange(maxlen, device=x.device) > pos
+        scores = scores.masked_fill(mask[None, :], float("-inf"))
+        p = torch.softmax(scores, dim=-1).to(torch.bfloat16)
+        pc = p @ c_kv_buf
+        o = torch.einsum("hd,hdc->hc", pc, self._Wvn)
+        of = o.reshape(H * vh).float()
+        return gemv(of, self.o_proj.w_q, self.o_proj.scales, self.o_proj.zeros).squeeze(0).to(torch.bfloat16)
+
