--- a//home/shadeform/mega/outputs/runs/20260618_170335_claude_claude-opus-4-8_03_kimi_linear_decode/repo/problems/03_kimi_linear_decode/solution.py
+++ b//home/shadeform/mega/outputs/runs/20260618_170335_claude_claude-opus-4-8_03_kimi_linear_decode/repo/problems/03_kimi_linear_decode/solution.py
@@ -412,13 +412,117 @@
         return h + self.moe.step(_rmsnorm(h, self.moe_norm))
 
 
+HEADROOM = 96
+
+
+class _Bundle:
+    """Persistent buffers + captured CUDA graph for one context length."""
+    __slots__ = ("maxlen", "h_in", "h_out", "pos", "S", "cq", "ck", "cv",
+                 "c_kv", "k_rope", "graph", "mla_idx")
+
+
 class Model(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self, cfg):
         super().__init__()
         self.cfg = cfg
         self.blocks = nn.ModuleList(Block(cfg, k) for k in cfg.pattern)
-
-    def step(self, hidden, state):
+        self._graphs = {}
+        self._use_graph = True
+
+    # ---- eager reference path (always correct) ---------------------------- #
+    def _step_eager(self, hidden, state):
         for i, blk in enumerate(self.blocks):
             hidden = blk.step(hidden, state[i])
         return hidden, state
+
+    # ---- graph machinery -------------------------------------------------- #
+    def _forward_graph(self, b: _Bundle):
+        cfg = self.cfg
+        x = b.h_in
+        ki = 0
+        for i, blk in enumerate(self.blocks):
+            xn = _rmsnorm(x, blk.attn_norm)
+            if blk.kind == "K":
+                a = blk.attn.step_g(xn, b.S[ki], b.cq[ki], b.ck[ki], b.cv[ki])
+                ki += 1
+            else:
+                a = blk.attn.step_g(xn, b.c_kv, b.k_rope, b.pos, b.maxlen)
+            h = x + a
+            x = h + blk.moe.step(_rmsnorm(h, blk.moe_norm))
+        b.h_out.copy_(x)
+        b.pos.add_(1)
+
+    def _make_bundle(self, ctx, device):
+        cfg = self.cfg
+        H, Dk = cfg.kda_heads, cfg.kda_head_dim
+        C = H * Dk
+        b = _Bundle()
+        b.maxlen = ctx + HEADROOM
+        b.h_in = torch.zeros(cfg.hidden, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        b.h_out = torch.zeros(cfg.hidden, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        b.pos = torch.zeros(1, device=device, dtype=torch.int64)
+        nk = sum(1 for k in cfg.pattern if k == "K")
+        b.S = [torch.zeros(H, Dk, Dk, device=device, dtype=torch.float32) for _ in range(nk)]
+        b.cq = [torch.zeros(3, C, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16) for _ in range(nk)]
+        b.ck = [torch.zeros(3, C, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16) for _ in range(nk)]
+        b.cv = [torch.zeros(3, C, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16) for _ in range(nk)]
+        b.c_kv = torch.zeros(b.maxlen, cfg.kv_lora, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        b.k_rope = torch.zeros(b.maxlen, cfg.qk_rope, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        b.mla_idx = cfg.pattern.index("M")
+        return b
+
+    def _capture(self, ctx, device):
+        b = self._make_bundle(ctx, device)
+        b.pos.fill_(ctx)
+        s = torch.cuda.Stream()
+        s.wait_stream(torch.cuda.current_stream())
+        with torch.cuda.stream(s):
+            for _ in range(3):
+                self._forward_graph(b)
+        torch.cuda.current_stream().wait_stream(s)
+        torch.cuda.synchronize()
+        b.graph = torch.cuda.CUDAGraph()
+        with torch.cuda.graph(b.graph):
+            self._forward_graph(b)
+        self._graphs[ctx] = b
+        return b
+
+    def _load_state(self, b, state, ctx):
+        """Copy a fresh dict state into bundle buffers; rebind dict to buffer views."""
+        ki = 0
+        for i, blk in enumerate(self.blocks):
+            st = state[i]
+            if blk.kind == "K":
+                b.S[ki].copy_(st["S"])
+                b.cq[ki].copy_(st["cq"]); b.ck[ki].copy_(st["ck"]); b.cv[ki].copy_(st["cv"])
+                st["S"] = b.S[ki]; st["cq"] = b.cq[ki]; st["ck"] = b.ck[ki]; st["cv"] = b.cv[ki]
+                ki += 1
+            else:
+                b.c_kv[:ctx].copy_(st["c_kv"]); b.k_rope[:ctx].copy_(st["k_rope"])
+                st["c_kv"] = b.c_kv[:ctx]; st["k_rope"] = b.k_rope[:ctx]
+        b.pos.fill_(ctx)
+
+    def step(self, hidden, state):
+        if not self._use_graph or not hidden.is_cuda:
+            return self._step_eager(hidden, state)
+        mla_idx = self.cfg.pattern.index("M")
+        ckv = state[mla_idx]["c_kv"]
+        try:
+            b = self._cur if getattr(self, "_cur", None) is not None else None
+            is_cont = (b is not None and ckv.data_ptr() == b.c_kv.data_ptr())
+            if not is_cont:
+                ctx = ckv.shape[0]
+                b = self._graphs.get(ctx) or self._capture(ctx, hidden.device)
+                self._load_state(b, state, ctx)
+                self._cur = b
+            b.h_in.copy_(hidden)
+            b.graph.replay()
+            # rebind dict views to current cache length
+            p = int(b.pos.item())
+            state[mla_idx]["c_kv"] = b.c_kv[:p]
+            state[mla_idx]["k_rope"] = b.k_rope[:p]
+            return b.h_out, state

     return out
 
 
+@triton.autotune(configs=_gemv_configs(), key=["N", "NG", "Eact"], reset_to_zero=["y_ptr"])
+@triton.jit
+def _gemv_acc_kernel(
+    x_ptr, wq_ptr, s_ptr, z_ptr, idx_ptr, sc_ptr, y_ptr,
+    K, N, NG, Eact,
+    stride_xe, stride_xk,
+    stride_we, stride_wk, stride_wn,
+    stride_se, stride_sg, stride_sn,
+    GROUP: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, SPLIT_K: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    """Weighted accumulate GEMV: y[n] += scale[e] * sum_k x[e,k]*w[e,k,n], over all e."""
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_e = tl.program_id(1)
+    pid_k = tl.program_id(2)
+    e = tl.load(idx_ptr + pid_e).to(tl.int64)
+    sc = tl.load(sc_ptr + pid_e)
+    n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    nmask = n < N
+    wq_e = wq_ptr + e * stride_we
+    s_e = s_ptr + e * stride_se
+    x_e = x_ptr + pid_e * stride_xe
+    acc = tl.zeros([BLOCK_N], dtype=tl.float32)
+    HG: tl.constexpr = GROUP // 2
+    rows = tl.arange(0, HG)
+    for g in range(pid_k, NG, SPLIT_K):
+        kp = g * HG + rows
+        wq = tl.load(wq_e + kp[:, None] * stride_wk + n[None, :] * stride_wn,
+                     mask=nmask[None, :], other=0)
+        lo = (wq & 0xF).to(tl.float32)
+        hi = ((wq >> 4) & 0xF).to(tl.float32)
+        xe_ = tl.load(x_e + (2 * kp) * stride_xk)
+        xo_ = tl.load(x_e + (2 * kp + 1) * stride_xk)
+        raw = tl.sum(xe_[:, None] * lo + xo_[:, None] * hi, axis=0)
+        xs = tl.sum(xe_ + xo_)
+        s = tl.load(s_e + g * stride_sg + n * stride_sn, mask=nmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        z = tl.load(s_e + (NG + g) * stride_sg + n * stride_sn, mask=nmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc += s * (raw - z * xs)
+    tl.atomic_add(y_ptr + n, sc * acc, mask=nmask)
+
+
+def gemv_acc(x, wq, scales, zeros, idx, scale, out):
+    """x:[Eact,K]; accumulate scale[e]*(x[e]@dequant(wq[idx[e]])) into out[N]."""
+    E, Kp, N = wq.shape
+    K = Kp * 2
+    NG = scales.shape[1]
+    Eact = idx.numel()
+    out.zero_()
+    # pack scales|zeros contiguously so kernel reads both from s_ptr (s at g, z at NG+g)
+    grid = lambda meta: (triton.cdiv(N, meta["BLOCK_N"]), Eact, meta["SPLIT_K"])
+    _gemv_acc_kernel[grid](
+        x, wq, scales, zeros, idx, scale, out,
+        K, N, NG, Eact,
+        x.stride(0), x.stride(1),
+        wq.stride(0), wq.stride(1), wq.stride(2),
+        scales.stride(0), scales.stride(1), scales.stride(2),
+        GROUP=GROUP,
+    )
+    return out
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _silu_mul_kernel(g_ptr, u_ptr, o_ptr, n_elem, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    off = pid * BLOCK + tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
+    m = off < n_elem
+    g = tl.load(g_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0)
+    u = tl.load(u_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0)
+    tl.store(o_ptr + off, (g * tl.sigmoid(g)) * u, mask=m)
+
+
+def silu_mul(g, u):
+    o = torch.empty_like(g)
+    n = g.numel()
+    _silu_mul_kernel[(triton.cdiv(n, 1024),)](g, u, o, n, BLOCK=1024)
+    return o
+
+

+@triton.jit
+def _rmsnorm_kernel(x_ptr, w_ptr, o_ptr, N: tl.constexpr, eps, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
+    off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
+    m = off < N
+    x = tl.load(x_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w = tl.load(w_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    r = tl.rsqrt(tl.sum(x * x) / N + eps)
+    tl.store(o_ptr + off, x * r * w, mask=m)
+
+

-    xf = x.float()
-    xf = xf * torch.rsqrt(xf.pow(2).mean(-1, keepdim=True) + EPS)
-    return (xf * w.float()).to(x.dtype)
+    """Fused RMSNorm; returns fp32 (ready for the dequant-GEMV)."""
+    N = x.shape[-1]
+    o = torch.empty(N, device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+    BLOCK = triton.next_power_of_2(N)
+    _rmsnorm_kernel[(1,)](x, w, o, N, EPS, BLOCK=BLOCK)
+    return o

+++ b//home/shadeform/.claude/projects/-home-shadeform-mega-outputs-runs-20260618-170335-claude-claude-opus-4-8-03-kimi-linear-decode/memory/kimi-linear-decode-optimization.md
@@ -0,0 +1,23 @@
+---
+name: kimi-linear-decode-optimization
+description: Key techniques + perf progression for the 03_kimi_linear_decode W4A16 megakernel problem
+metadata:
+  type: project
+---
+
+Problem: make batch-1 W4A16 Kimi-Linear hybrid decode fast vs baseline.py. Score = geomean speedup over ctx 2048/8192/16384. Correctness gate: `python check.py` must print PASS (cos>=0.98). Run via `uv run python check.py` / `uv run python benchmark.py` (the bare `python` wrapper lacks torch).
+
+Actual GPU is a **B200** (not RTX PRO 6000), ~6-7 TB/s achievable copy bw, but small (5-20MB) GEMVs only hit ~1-1.8 TB/s (overhead/latency bound). Per-kernel GPU floor ~2-3us.
+
+What worked (perf progression):
+- Fused int4 dequant-GEMV (Triton, split-K + atomics, group xsum trick) → 3x
+- **autotune gotcha**: atomic-accumulate kernels corrupt on first call unless `reset_to_zero=["y_ptr"]` is set (autotuner benchmarks many configs onto same buffer, then the real run atomic-adds onto garbage). Keep per-call `out.zero_()` too (cached path skips reset_to_zero).
+- MLA absorb (precompute kv_b dequant ONCE into per-head bf16 Wkn/Wvn; scores as [H,L] so softmax is over contiguous last dim — `softmax(dim=0)` of [L,H] was 1.1ms/step "spatial softmax"!) + bf16 tensor-core matmuls over cache
+- batch KDA q/k/v/g into one gemv; fused KDA gated-delta recurrence kernel (one program per head, S updated in place)
+- **CUDA graphs** (biggest single win, 3.4x→7.2x): fixed-size MLA cache buffer [ctx+HEADROOM,512] + GPU `pos` scalar, mask cols>pos, index_copy_ new row at pos. New-run detection by data_ptr; CPU-side `cpos` counter avoids per-step pos.item() sync. Fall back to eager on exception.
+- Fused MoE: combine routed+shared experts (cat weight buffers, gather index includes shared at index n_experts), silu_mul kernel, weighted-accumulate down GEMV (gemv_acc: scale[e]*acc atomic-added to single [hidden] out) → 8.1x
+- Fused RMSNorm kernel returning fp32 directly (cast beta_proj/router inputs to bf16) → 9.3x
+
+Backups: solution_vN_*.py.bak. Dev scripts: dev_*.py.
+
+Next targets: fuse conv (memcpy+elementwise), fuse rope, reduce gemv zero_ launches, maybe fuse KDA prep (softplus/sigmoid) into recurrence.

 @triton.jit
+def _kda_conv_kernel(
+    qkv_ptr, cw_ptr, st_ptr, out_ptr, C,
+    scw_t, scw_n, scw_k, BLOCK: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    """Depthwise causal conv (kernel 4) + SiLU on q/k/v, with in-place ring shift.
+    qkv_ptr: [>=3, C] (rows q,k,v); st_ptr: [3,3,C] window state; out_ptr: [3,C]."""
+    pid_t = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
+    n = pid_n * BLOCK + tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
+    m = n < C
+    val = tl.load(qkv_ptr + pid_t * C + n, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    cw = cw_ptr + pid_t * scw_t + n * scw_n
+    w0 = tl.load(cw + 0 * scw_k, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w1 = tl.load(cw + 1 * scw_k, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w2 = tl.load(cw + 2 * scw_k, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w3 = tl.load(cw + 3 * scw_k, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    sb = st_ptr + pid_t * 3 * C + n
+    s0 = tl.load(sb + 0 * C, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    s1 = tl.load(sb + 1 * C, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    s2 = tl.load(sb + 2 * C, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    acc = s0 * w0 + s1 * w1 + s2 * w2 + val * w3
+    tl.store(out_ptr + pid_t * C + n, acc * tl.sigmoid(acc), mask=m)
+    tl.store(sb + 0 * C, s1.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=m)
+    tl.store(sb + 1 * C, s2.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=m)
+    tl.store(sb + 2 * C, val.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=m)
+
+
+def kda_conv(qkv, conv_w, state):
+    """qkv:[>=3,C]; conv_w:[3,C,4]; state:[3,3,C] bf16 (in place). -> out:[3,C] fp32."""
+    C = qkv.shape[1]
+    out = torch.empty((3, C), device=qkv.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+    grid = (3, triton.cdiv(C, 1024))
+    _kda_conv_kernel[grid](
+        qkv, conv_w, state, out, C,
+        conv_w.stride(0), conv_w.stride(1), conv_w.stride(2), BLOCK=1024,
+    )
+    return out
+
+

361	    def _conv(self, val, prev, idx):
362	        # val:[C] fp32, prev:[3,C] bf16, conv_w[idx]:[C,4]
363	        win = torch.cat([prev.float(), val[None]], dim=0)      # [4,C]
364	        w = self.conv_w[idx].float().transpose(0, 1)            # [4,C]
365	        out = F.silu((win * w).sum(0))                          # [C]
366	        return out, win[1:].to(prev.dtype)
367	
368	    def step(self, x, st):
369	        H, Dk = self.cfg.kda_heads, self.cfg.kda_head_dim
370	        if not hasattr(self, "_wq"):
371	            self._stack()
372	        xf = x.float()
373	        qkvg = gemv(xf, self._wq, self._s, self._z)            # [4, H*Dk]
374	        q, st["cq"] = self._conv(qkvg[0], st["cq"], 0)
375	        k, st["ck"] = self._conv(qkvg[1], st["ck"], 1)
376	        v, st["cv"] = self._conv(qkvg[2], st["cv"], 2)
377	        q = (q.view(H, Dk) * self.scale).contiguous()
378	        k = k.view(H, Dk).contiguous()
379	        v = v.view(H, Dk).contiguous()

381	        beta = torch.sigmoid(self.beta_proj(x.to(torch.bfloat16)).float()).contiguous()

383	        of = o.reshape(H * Dk)

545	class _Bundle:
546	    """Persistent buffers + captured CUDA graph for one context length."""
547	    __slots__ = ("maxlen", "h_in", "h_out", "pos", "cpos", "S", "cq", "ck", "cv",
548	                 "c_kv", "k_rope", "graph", "mla_idx")
549	
550	
551	class Model(nn.Module):
552	    def __init__(self, cfg):
553	        super().__init__()
554	        self.cfg = cfg
555	        self.blocks = nn.ModuleList(Block(cfg, k) for k in cfg.pattern)
556	        self._graphs = {}
557	        self._use_graph = True
558	
559	    # ---- eager reference path (always correct) ---------------------------- #
560	    def _step_eager(self, hidden, state):
561	        for i, blk in enumerate(self.blocks):
562	            hidden = blk.step(hidden, state[i])
563	        return hidden, state
564	
565	    # ---- graph machinery -------------------------------------------------- #
566	    def _forward_graph(self, b: _Bundle):
567	        cfg = self.cfg
568	        x = b.h_in
569	        ki = 0
570	        for i, blk in enumerate(self.blocks):
571	            xn = _rmsnorm(x, blk.attn_norm)
572	            if blk.kind == "K":
573	                a = blk.attn.step_g(xn, b.S[ki], b.cq[ki], b.ck[ki], b.cv[ki])
574	                ki += 1
575	            else:
576	                a = blk.attn.step_g(xn, b.c_kv, b.k_rope, b.pos, b.maxlen)
577	            h = x + a
578	            x = h + blk.moe.step(_rmsnorm(h, blk.moe_norm))
579	        b.h_out.copy_(x)
580	        b.pos.add_(1)

import torch, triton, triton.language as tl
import reference as R
from solution import gemv as gemv_cur

dev="cuda"
def gpu(fn,it=400):
    for _ in range(40): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize(); s=torch.cuda.Event(True); e=torch.cuda.Event(True); s.record()
    for _ in range(it): fn()
    e.record(); torch.cuda.synchronize(); return s.elapsed_time(e)/it*1e3

# real shapes: qkvg E4 (2304->4096), MLA q E1 (2304->6144), o E1(4096->2304), moe gate E9 (2304->1024)
def mk(E,Kin,N):
    wq=torch.randint(0,255,(E,Kin//2,N),device=dev,dtype=torch.uint8)
    sc=torch.randn(E,Kin//128,N,device=dev,dtype=torch.bfloat16).abs()*0.01
    ze=torch.randint(0,15,(E,Kin//128,N),device=dev).to(torch.bfloat16)
    return wq,sc,ze
cases=[("qkvg",4,2304,4096),("mla_q",1,2304,6144),("kda_o",1,4096,2304),("moe_gate",9,2304,1024),("moe_down",9,1024,2304)]
for name,E,Kin,N in cases:
    wq,sc,ze=mk(E,Kin,N)
    x=torch.randn(Kin,device=dev,dtype=torch.float32) if E==1 else torch.randn(Kin,device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
    idx=torch.arange(E,device=dev,dtype=torch.int32) if E>1 else None
    if E>1 and name=="moe_down":
        x=torch.randn(E,Kin,device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
    mb=E*Kin*N*0.5/1e6
    t=gpu(lambda: gemv_cur(x,wq,sc,ze,idx=idx))
    print(f"{name:10s} E={E} ({mb:.1f}MB): {t:.2f}us  {mb/t:.2f}TB/s")

Every eager gemv is a uniform ~20 µs (launch+zero floor), so eager micro-bench is misleading — in-graph the kernel is ~11.5 µs avg (~0.9 TB/s on 218 MB). That's the biggest lever (242 µs). Let me do a proper **in-graph config search** on the real shapes to find optimal configs, then hardcode them (also speeds up capture by dropping autotune).

cat > dev_search.py << 'EOF'
import torch, triton, triton.language as tl
dev="cuda"
# minimal standalone kernel = copy of solution's _gemv_kernel body, with explicit config
@triton.jit
def _k(x_ptr,wq_ptr,s_ptr,z_ptr,idx_ptr,y_ptr,K,N,NG,Eact,
       sxe,sxk,swe,swk,swn,sse,ssg,ssn,sye,syn,
       GROUP:tl.constexpr,USE_IDX:tl.constexpr,BLOCK_N:tl.constexpr,SPLIT_K:tl.constexpr):
    pid_n=tl.program_id(0);pid_e=tl.program_id(1);pid_k=tl.program_id(2)
    e=tl.load(idx_ptr+pid_e).to(tl.int64) if USE_IDX else pid_e
    n=pid_n*BLOCK_N+tl.arange(0,BLOCK_N);nm=n<N
    wq_e=wq_ptr+e*swe; s_e=s_ptr+e*sse; z_e=z_ptr+e*sse; x_e=x_ptr+pid_e*sxe
    acc=tl.zeros([BLOCK_N],dtype=tl.float32); HG:tl.constexpr=GROUP//2; rows=tl.arange(0,HG)
    for g in range(pid_k,NG,SPLIT_K):
        kp=g*HG+rows
        wq=tl.load(wq_e+kp[:,None]*swk+n[None,:]*swn,mask=nm[None,:],other=0)
        lo=(wq&0xF).to(tl.float32);hi=((wq>>4)&0xF).to(tl.float32)
        xe_=tl.load(x_e+(2*kp)*sxk);xo_=tl.load(x_e+(2*kp+1)*sxk)
        raw=tl.sum(xe_[:,None]*lo+xo_[:,None]*hi,axis=0);xs=tl.sum(xe_+xo_)
        s=tl.load(s_e+g*ssg+n*ssn,mask=nm,other=0.).to(tl.float32)
        z=tl.load(z_e+g*ssg+n*ssn,mask=nm,other=0.).to(tl.float32)
        acc+=s*(raw-z*xs)
    if SPLIT_K==1: tl.store(y_ptr+pid_e*sye+n*syn,acc,mask=nm)
    else: tl.atomic_add(y_ptr+pid_e*sye+n*syn,acc,mask=nm)

def run(x,wq,sc,ze,out,idx,BN,SK,nw,ns):
    E,Kp,N=wq.shape; K=Kp*2; NG=sc.shape[1]; Eact=idx.numel() if idx is not None else E
    sxe,sxk=(0,x.stride(0)) if x.dim()==1 else (x.stride(0),x.stride(1))
    out.zero_()
    _k[(triton.cdiv(N,BN),Eact,SK)](x,wq,sc,ze, idx if idx is not None else x, out,K,N,NG,Eact,
        sxe,sxk,wq.stride(0),wq.stride(1),wq.stride(2),sc.stride(0),sc.stride(1),sc.stride(2),
        out.stride(0),out.stride(1),GROUP=128,USE_IDX=idx is not None,BLOCK_N=BN,SPLIT_K=SK,num_warps=nw,num_stages=ns)

def graphtime(fn,it=200):
    for _ in range(5): fn()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    s=torch.cuda.Stream(); s.wait_stream(torch.cuda.current_stream())
    with torch.cuda.stream(s):
        for _ in range(3): fn()
    torch.cuda.current_stream().wait_stream(s)
    g=torch.cuda.CUDAGraph()
    with torch.cuda.graph(g): fn()
    ev1=torch.cuda.Event(True);ev2=torch.cuda.Event(True);ev1.record()
    for _ in range(it): g.replay()
    ev2.record();torch.cuda.synchronize(); return ev1.elapsed_time(ev2)/it*1e3

def mk(E,Kin,N):
    return (torch.randint(0,255,(E,Kin//2,N),device=dev,dtype=torch.uint8),
            torch.randn(E,Kin//128,N,device=dev,dtype=torch.bfloat16).abs()*0.01,
            torch.randint(0,15,(E,Kin//128,N),device=dev).to(torch.bfloat16))
cases=[("qkvg",4,2304,4096),("mla_q",1,2304,6144),("kda_o",1,4096,2304),("moe_gate",9,2304,1024),("moe_down",9,1024,2304)]
for name,E,Kin,N in cases:
    wq,sc,ze=mk(E,Kin,N)
    x=torch.randn(E,Kin,device=dev,dtype=torch.float32) if name=="moe_down" else torch.randn(Kin,device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
    idx=torch.arange(E,device=dev,dtype=torch.int32) if E>1 else None
    out=torch.empty((E if idx is None else idx.numel(),N),device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
    mb=E*Kin*N*0.5/1e6; best=(None,1e9)
    for BN in [32,64,128,256]:
        for SK in [1,2,4,8,16]:
            for nw in [1,2,4,8]:
                for ns in [2,3,4]:
                    try: t=graphtime(lambda BN=BN,SK=SK,nw=nw,ns=ns: run(x,wq,sc,ze,out,idx,BN,SK,nw,ns))
                    except Exception: continue
                    if t<best[1]: best=((BN,SK,nw,ns),t)
    print(f"{name:9s} ({mb:.1f}MB): best {best[0]} {best[1]:.2f}us {mb/best[1]:.2f}TB/s")
EOF

399	class MLA(nn.Module):
400	    def __init__(self, cfg):
401	        super().__init__()
402	        self.cfg = cfg
403	        H, d = cfg.mla_heads, cfg.hidden
404	        self.q_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope), cfg.group)
405	        self.kv_a = QuantLinear(d, cfg.kv_lora + cfg.qk_rope, cfg.group)
406	        self.kv_b = QuantLinear(cfg.kv_lora, H * (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.v_head), cfg.group)
407	        self.o_proj = QuantLinear(H * cfg.v_head, d, cfg.group)
408	        self.scale = (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope) ** -0.5
409	
410	    def _prep(self):
411	        cfg = self.cfg
412	        H, nope, vh, lora = cfg.mla_heads, cfg.qk_nope, cfg.v_head, cfg.kv_lora
413	        W = _unpack_dequant(self.kv_b.w_q, self.kv_b.scales, self.kv_b.zeros).view(lora, H, nope + vh)
414	        # per-head absorb matrices, bf16 for tensor-core matmuls
415	        self._Wkn = W[:, :, :nope].permute(1, 0, 2).contiguous()   # [H,512,nope]
416	        self._Wvn = W[:, :, nope:].permute(1, 0, 2).contiguous()   # [H,512,vh]
417	        dev = self.kv_b.w_q.device

     return o
 
 
+@triton.jit
+def _rmsnorm_add_kernel(x_ptr, y_ptr, w_ptr, resid_ptr, o_ptr, N: tl.constexpr, eps, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
+    off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
+    m = off < N
+    s = tl.load(x_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32) + tl.load(y_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    tl.store(resid_ptr + off, s.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=m)
+    r = tl.rsqrt(tl.sum(s * s) / N + eps)
+    w = tl.load(w_ptr + off, mask=m, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    tl.store(o_ptr + off, s * r * w, mask=m)
+
+
+def _rmsnorm_add(x, y, w):
+    """resid = x + y (bf16); returns (resid, rmsnorm(resid) fp32)."""
+    N = x.shape[-1]
+    resid = torch.empty(N, device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    o = torch.empty(N, device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+    _rmsnorm_add_kernel[(1,)](x, y, w, resid, o, N, EPS, BLOCK=triton.next_power_of_2(N))
+    return resid, o
+
+

16.28×. The MoE routing (topk gather 21 µs + cats 20 µs + softmax 6 µs + router matmul) is the last big clean chunk (~50 µs). Let me write a fused router+top-k kernel that computes logits, selects top-8, softmaxes, and emits the gather indices directly — eliminating ~6 ops/MoE. This is register-based to avoid store-then-load hazards:

--- a//home/shadeform/mega/outputs/runs/20260618_170335_claude_claude-opus-4-8_03_kimi_linear_decode/repo/problems/03_kimi_linear_decode/solution.py
+++ b//home/shadeform/mega/outputs/runs/20260618_170335_claude_claude-opus-4-8_03_kimi_linear_decode/repo/problems/03_kimi_linear_decode/solution.py
@@ -173,6 +173,64 @@
 
 
 @triton.jit
+def _router_topk_kernel(
+    x_ptr, w_ptr, idxg_ptr, idxgu_ptr, scale_ptr,
+    D, E, scaling, GATE_OFF,
+    NACT: tl.constexpr, NS: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_E: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_J: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    """Fused router GEMV + top-k(logits) + softmax + gather-index build (one program).
+    Emits idx_g[NACT+NS], idx_gu[2*(NACT+NS)] (gate then up), scale[NACT+NS]."""
+    e = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_E)
+    emask = e < E
+    logits = tl.zeros([BLOCK_E], dtype=tl.float32)
+    for d0 in range(0, D, BLOCK_D):
+        dd = d0 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_D)
+        dmask = dd < D
+        xv = tl.load(x_ptr + dd, mask=dmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        wv = tl.load(w_ptr + e[:, None] * D + dd[None, :],
+                     mask=emask[:, None] & dmask[None, :], other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        logits += tl.sum(wv * xv[None, :], axis=1)
+    logits = tl.where(emask, logits, -float("inf"))
+    jr = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_J)
+    idx_vec = tl.zeros([BLOCK_J], dtype=tl.int32)
+    val_vec = tl.full([BLOCK_J], -float("inf"), dtype=tl.float32)
+    for j in range(NACT):
+        mx = tl.max(logits, 0)
+        am = tl.argmax(logits, 0).to(tl.int32)
+        idx_vec = tl.where(jr == j, am, idx_vec)
+        val_vec = tl.where(jr == j, mx, val_vec)
+        logits = tl.where(e == am, -float("inf"), logits)
+    idx_vec = tl.where(jr == NACT, E, idx_vec)               # shared expert at slot NACT
+    routed = jr < NACT
+    vmax = tl.max(tl.where(routed, val_vec, -float("inf")), 0)
+    ev = tl.where(routed, tl.exp(val_vec - vmax), 0.0)
+    sm = ev / tl.sum(ev, 0) * scaling
+    scale_vec = tl.where(routed, sm, tl.where(jr == NACT, 1.0, 0.0))
+    ns_mask = jr < (NACT + NS)
+    tl.store(idxg_ptr + jr, idx_vec, mask=ns_mask)
+    tl.store(scale_ptr + jr, scale_vec, mask=ns_mask)
+    tl.store(idxgu_ptr + jr, idx_vec, mask=ns_mask)
+    tl.store(idxgu_ptr + (NACT + NS) + jr, idx_vec + GATE_OFF, mask=ns_mask)
+
+
+def router_topk(x, w, n_active, n_shared, gate_off, scaling, E):
+    dev = x.device
+    ns = n_active + n_shared
+    idx_g = torch.empty(ns, device=dev, dtype=torch.int32)
+    idx_gu = torch.empty(2 * ns, device=dev, dtype=torch.int32)
+    scale = torch.empty(ns, device=dev, dtype=torch.float32)
+    D = x.shape[-1]
+    BLOCK_J = triton.next_power_of_2(ns)
+    _router_topk_kernel[(1,)](
+        x, w, idx_g, idx_gu, scale, D, E, scaling, gate_off,
+        NACT=n_active, NS=n_shared,
+        BLOCK_D=256, BLOCK_E=triton.next_power_of_2(E), BLOCK_J=BLOCK_J,
+    )
+    return idx_g, idx_gu, scale
+
+
+@triton.jit
 def _silu_mul_kernel(g_ptr, u_ptr, o_ptr, n_elem, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
     pid = tl.program_id(0)
     off = pid * BLOCK + tl.arange(0, BLOCK)

--- a//home/shadeform/mega/outputs/runs/20260618_170335_claude_claude-opus-4-8_03_kimi_linear_decode/repo/problems/03_kimi_linear_decode/solution.py
+++ b//home/shadeform/mega/outputs/runs/20260618_170335_claude_claude-opus-4-8_03_kimi_linear_decode/repo/problems/03_kimi_linear_decode/solution.py
@@ -173,25 +173,30 @@
 
 
 @triton.jit
+def _router_logits_kernel(x_ptr, w_ptr, out_ptr, D, BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr):
+    """One program per expert: logit[e] = sum_d x[d] * W[e,d]."""
+    e = tl.program_id(0)
+    acc = tl.zeros([BLOCK_D], dtype=tl.float32)
+    for d0 in range(0, D, BLOCK_D):
+        dd = d0 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_D)
+        dm = dd < D
+        acc += tl.load(x_ptr + dd, mask=dm, other=0.0).to(tl.float32) * \
+            tl.load(w_ptr + e * D + dd, mask=dm, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    tl.store(out_ptr + e, tl.sum(acc, 0))
+
+
+@triton.jit
 def _router_topk_kernel(
-    x_ptr, w_ptr, idxg_ptr, idxgu_ptr, scale_ptr,
-    D, E, scaling, GATE_OFF,
+    logits_ptr, idxg_ptr, idxgu_ptr, scale_ptr,
+    E, scaling, GATE_OFF,

Done. ## Summary I built `solution.py` — a fused W4A16 Kimi-Linear hybrid decode kernel that runs at **~0.46–0.49 ms/tok (~2100 tok/s), ~19× faster than `baseline.py`**, passing `check.py` (cosine ≥ 0.9947, well above the 0.98 gate). The GPU is actually a **B200** (Blackwell, ~6–7 TB/s), so this decode is dominated by per-kernel launch/floor overhead, not just raw bandwidth. The optimizations, in order of impact: **Core requirement — fused int4 dequant-GEMV (Triton):** streams the int4 weights once and fuses unpack + per-group asymmetric dequant directly into the GEMV using the group identity `y = Σ_g s_g·(Σ x·w − z_g·Σx)`, with split-K + atomics and autotuned configs. Never materializes the bf16 weight (2.5× faster than torch's bf16 GEMV per effective weight, at ¼ the bytes). **MLA absorb:** precompute the `kv_b` dequant **once** into per-head bf16 matrices; reformulate so the latent cache is never re-expanded, and keep scores as `[H, L]` so softmax is over the contiguous last dim (the reference's `softmax(dim=0)` over the strided 16k axis was 1.1 ms/step alone). **CUDA graphs (biggest single win, 3.4×→7.2×):** fixed-size MLA cache buffer + GPU `pos` scalar (masked attention, in-place `index_copy_`), eliminating ~1.4 ms/step of CPU launch overhead. New-run detection by `data_ptr`; eager fallback verified correct. **Aggressive fusion** of everything else: gated-delta recurrence kernel (with `exp(-softplus)=sigmoid(-x)` folded in), depthwise conv kernel, RMSNorm-fused-with-residual-add, combined gate‖up and q_proj‖kv_a GEMVs, weighted-accumulate down-projection, and a fused router top-k that emits gather indices directly. The remaining bottleneck is the int4 GEMV stream itself (~217 µs, 50% of the step) — floor-bound on 16 sequentially-dependent kernels. Going further would require a single persistent megakernel with grid-wide sync, which I judged too high-risk for the marginal gain given the already-strong, robust result.
